[[File:Damage in Gaza Strip during the October 2023 - 13.jpg|thumb|305px|Residents inspect the ruins of an apartment destroyed by Israeli airstrikes|alt=People stand amid the rubble of a building and looking at the ground. A man is carrying a large flower-patterned object.]]
{{Campaignbox Gaza war}}
{{Campaignbox Gaza–Israel conflict}}

The [[Gaza Strip]] is experiencing a [[humanitarian crisis]] as a result of the [[Gaza war]].<ref name="spiraling humanitarian crisis">{{cite web |last1=Ioanes |first1=Ellen |title=Gaza's spiraling humanitarian crisis, explained |url=https://www.vox.com/2023/10/14/23917260/israel-hamas-war-gaza-humanitarian-crisis |work=[[Vox (website)|Vox]] |date=14 October 2023 |access-date=16 October 2023 |archive-date=14 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231014224531/https://www.vox.com/2023/10/14/23917260/israel-hamas-war-gaza-humanitarian-crisis |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="humanitarian catastrophe">{{cite news |last1=Marsi |first1=Federica |title=Gaza doctors warn of a humanitarian catastrophe after Israeli attacks |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/14/supplies-exhausted-doctors-exhausted-in-gaza-catastrophe-looms-large |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |date=14 October 2023 |access-date=25 October 2023 |archive-date=14 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231014174402/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/14/supplies-exhausted-doctors-exhausted-in-gaza-catastrophe-looms-large |url-status=live}}</ref> The crisis includes both an impending [[Gaza Strip famine|famine]] and a [[Timeline of the Gaza Strip healthcare collapse|healthcare collapse]]. At the start of the [[war]], Israel tightened its [[October 2023 Israeli blockade of the Gaza Strip|blockade on the Gaza Strip]], which has resulted in significant shortages of fuel, food, medication, water, and essential medical supplies.<ref name="spiraling humanitarian crisis" /><ref>{{cite web |last1=Gottbrath |first1=Laurin-Whitney |title=Gaza "fast becoming hell hole" on "brink of collapse" amid Israel strikes: UN |url=https://www.axios.com/2023/10/14/gaza-humanitarian-crisis-hamas-israel-war-death-toll |work=[[Axios (website)|Axios]] |date=14 October 2023 |access-date=16 October 2023 |archive-date=16 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231016101000/https://www.axios.com/2023/10/14/gaza-humanitarian-crisis-hamas-israel-war-death-toll |url-status=live}}</ref> This siege resulted in a 90% drop in electricity availability, impacting hospital power supplies, sewage plants, and shutting down the desalination plants that provide drinking water.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Mellen |first1=Ruby |last2=Chen |first2=Szu Yu |title=See how Israel's siege has plunged Gaza into darkness and isolation |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]] |date=26 October 2023 |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/10/26/gaza-israel-siege-blackout-isolation/ |access-date=27 October 2023 |archive-date=27 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231027220800/https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/10/26/gaza-israel-siege-blackout-isolation/ |url-status=live}}</ref> Doctors warned of disease outbreaks spreading due to overcrowded hospitals.<ref name="humanitarian catastrophe" />

Heavy bombardment by Israeli airstrikes caused catastrophic damage to Gaza’s infrastructure, further deepening the crisis.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/gaza-war-inflicts-catastrophic-damage-infrastructure-economy-2023-11-17/ |title=Gaza war inflicts catastrophic damage on infrastructure and economy |date=21 November 2023 |work=[[Reuters]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231130145841/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/gaza-war-inflicts-catastrophic-damage-infrastructure-economy-2023-11-17/ |archive-date=30 November 2023}}</ref> The [[Gaza Health Ministry]] reported over 4,000 children killed in the war's first month.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Al-Mughrabi |first1=Nidal |title=Gaza death toll tops 10,000; UN calls it a children's graveyard |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/pressure-israel-over-civilians-steps-up-ceasefire-calls-rebuffed-2023-11-06/ |work=[[Reuters]] |date=6 November 2023 |access-date=8 November 2023 |archive-date=7 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231107235020/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/pressure-israel-over-civilians-steps-up-ceasefire-calls-rebuffed-2023-11-06/ |url-status=live}}</ref> UN Secretary General [[António Guterres]] stated Gaza had "become a graveyard for children."{{efn|Israeli UN Ambassador [[Gilad Erdan]] responded directly to Guterres, stating, "Shame on [Guterres]... More than 30 minors – among them a 9-month-old baby as well as toddlers and children who witnessed their parents being murdered in cold blood – are being held against their will in the Gaza Strip. Hamas is the problem in Gaza, not Israel's actions to eliminate this terrorist organization."<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/live/world-middle-east-67324897 |work=[[BBC News]] |date=6 November 2023 |title=UN says Gaza becoming |access-date=7 November 2023 |archive-date=7 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231107033550/https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/live/world-middle-east-67324897 |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |title=UN chief: Gaza has become 'graveyard for kids'; Israeli envoy calls for him to resign |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/un-chief-gaza-has-become-graveyard-for-kids-israeli-envoy-urges-his-resignation/#:~:text=Israel%27s%20Ambassador%20to%20the%20United,held%20in%20the%20Gaza%20Strip. |url-status=live}}</ref>}}<ref>{{cite news |last1=Nichols |first1=Michelle |title=UN chief says Gaza becoming a 'graveyard for children' [[Samantha Power]] stated that conditions in Gaza were "worse than ever before".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Suter |first1=Tara |title=Gaza conditions worse than ever, USAID chief says |url=https://thehill.com/homenews/administration/4693423-usaid-samantha-power-gaza-rafah-conditions-israel-hamas-war/ |work=[[The Hill (newspaper)|The Hill]] |access-date=8 June 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240531212821/https://thehill.com/homenews/administration/4693423-usaid-samantha-power-gaza-rafah-conditions-israel-hamas-war/ |archive-date=31 May 2024}}</ref>

Organizations such as [[Doctors Without Borders]], the [[Red Cross]], and a joint statement by [[UNICEF]], the World Health Organization, the [[UN Development Programme]], [[United Nations Population Fund]], and [[World Food Programme]] have warned of a dire humanitarian collapse.<ref>{{cite tweet |author=Doctors w/o Borders |user=MSF_USA |number=1715416018594529450 |date=20 October 2023 |title=You need that fuel to run generators for life-saving medical equipment.' There is a lack of painkillers. Access to supplies means life or death at this point. We're deeply concerned for the fate of everyone in Gaza right now. |access-date=20 October 2023}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |title='The world must do more' for Gaza, 5 UN agencies say |url=https://news.un.org/en/story/2023/10/1142652 |work=UN News |date=21 October 2023 |access-date=22 October 2023 |archive-date=21 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231021191654/https://news.un.org/en/story/2023/10/1142652 |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |first1=Umut |last1=Uras |first2=Priyanka |last2=Shankar |first3=Mersiha |last3=Gadzo |title=Red Cross president says 'shocked by the intolerable level of human suffering' |url=https://aje.io/nw7juv?update=2445050 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=28 October 2023 |archive-date=28 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231028211136/https://aje.io/nw7juv?update=2445050 |url-status=live}}</ref>

== Background ==
According to diplomats, [[Hamas]] had repeatedly said in the months leading up to [[7 October Hamas-led attack on Israel|7 October 2023]] that it did not want another military escalation in Gaza as it would worsen the humanitarian crisis that occurred after the [[2021 Israel–Palestine crisis|2021 conflict]].<ref name=":5">{{#invoke:cite news||last=Abdulrahim |first=Raja |date=7 October 2023 |title=Gaza Has Suffered Under 16-Year Blockade |work=[[The New York Times]] |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/10/07/world/middleeast/gaza-blockade-israel.html |access-date=16 October 2023 |archive-date=24 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231024053734/https://www.nytimes.com/2023/10/07/world/middleeast/gaza-blockade-israel.html |url-status=live}}</ref>

== Food and water ==
=== Impending famine ===
{{main|Gaza Strip famine}}

The situation in the Gaza Strip reached dire levels of starvation and food insecurity by late 2023 and early 2024. Reports from various sources including the [[World Food Programme]] and [[United Nations]] officials highlighted a devastating situation where food stocks were nearly exhausted, bakeries were being destroyed by Israeli airstrikes, and access to basic food supplies became increasingly scarce.<ref>{{bulleted list|

As the conflict persisted, the Gaza Strip has been pushed to the brink of famine,<ref>{{cite news |last1=Vinall |first1=Frances |title='Immediate possibility of starvation' in Gaza, World Food Program international aid organizations and relief workers sounded alarms of mass starvation, with the majority of households facing inadequate food consumption and a significant portion resorting to extreme By early 2024, the Gaza Strip faced one of the worst instances of man-made starvation in a century.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Nolen |first1=Stephanie |title=Looming Starvation in Gaza Shows Resurgence of Civilian Sieges in Warfare |work=[[The New York Times]] |date=11 January 2024 |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2024/01/11/health/gaza-israel-hunger-starvation.html |access-date=14 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240301042147/https://www.nytimes.com/2024/01/11/health/gaza-israel-hunger-starvation.html |archive-date=1 March 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Stack |first1=Liam |last2=Gupta |first2=Gaya |last3=Abu Bakr |first3=Bashir |title=Half of Gazans Are at Risk of Starving, U.N. the severity of the crisis.<ref>{{cite magazine |last1=Chotiner |first1=Isaac |title=Gaza Is Starving |url=https://www.newyorker.com/news/q-and-a/gaza-is-starving |magazine=[[The New Yorker]] |date=3 |archive-date=13 February 2024}}</ref> The international community expressed grave concerns, acknowledging the pervasive shadow of starvation looming over the people of Gaza and underscoring the |archive-date=9 January 2024}}</ref> 2.2 million people in Gaza are considered to be experiencing food insecurity at the emergency level.<ref>{{cite web |url=https://www.redcross.org.uk/stories/disasters-and-emergencies/world/whats-happening-in-gaza-humanitarian-crisis-grows |title=Summary of events in Gaza |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240409172618/https://www.redcross.org.uk/stories/disasters-and-emergencies/world/whats-happening-in-gaza-humanitarian-crisis-grows |archive-date=9 April 2024 |access-date=13 February 2024}}</ref>

Israel has challenged the IPC's past methodology, citing academics in the Israeli public health sector.<ref>{{cite news |last=Sharon |first=Jeremy |date=31 May 2024 |title=Key Gaza famine report cited by UN, ICJ has systematic flaws, Israeli review finds |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/key-gaza-famine-report-cited-by-un-icj-has-systematic-flaws-israeli-review-finds/ |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240531191656/https://www.timesofisrael.com/key-gaza-famine-report-cited-by-un-icj-has-systematic-flaws-israeli-review-finds/ |archive-date=31 May 2024}}</ref> An independent study by researchers from [[Columbia University]] found that "sufficient amounts of food are being supplied into Gaza", though, "it may not always be distributed to people due to other factors, such as war and Hamas control".<ref>{{cite news |date=18 June 2024 |title=Experts: ICC and UN blamed Israel for a famine that never happened in Gaza - exclusive |url=https://www.jpost.com/israel-hamas-war/article-806739 |access-date=27 June 2024 |work=[[The Jerusalem Post]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240627102901/https://www.jpost.com/israel-hamas-war/article-806739 |archive-date=27 June 2024}}</ref>

According to a letter sent to President [[Joseph R. Biden]], Vice President [[Kamala D. Harris]], and others on October 2, 2024 by 99 American healthcare workers who have served in the Gaza Strip since October 7, 2023, and cited in a study from the [[Watson Institute for International and Public Affairs]] at [[Brown University]], based on starvation standards by the United States-funded [[Integrated Food Security Phase Classification]], according to the most conservative estimate that they could calculate based on the available data, at least 62,413 people in Gaza have thus far died from starvation, most of them young children.<ref name="MotherJonesTotalDeaths">{{cite web |url=https://www.motherjones.com/politics/2024/10/us-israel-funding-gaza-palestine-deaths-october-100000-17-billion/ |title=Report: In One Year, More Than 100,000 Deaths in Gaza—Aided by $17.9 Billion From the US |last=Hurwitz |first=Sophie |date=8 October 2024 |website=[[Mother Jones (magazine)|Mother Jones]] |access-date=17 October 2024 |quote=Brown University’s Costs of War Project calculated “the money that’s spent on war, and the toll on human lives” after a year of war in Gaza. The numbers are staggering.}}</ref><ref name="WatsonInstituteEstimatedDeaths">{{cite web |url=https://watson.brown.edu/costsofwar/files/cow/imce/papers/2023/2024/Costs%20of%20War_Human%20Toll%20Since%20Oct%207.pdf |title=The Human Toll: Indirect Deaths from War in Gaza and the West Bank, October 7, 2023 Forward |last=Stamatopoulou-Robbins |first=Sophia |date=7 October 2024 |publisher=[[Watson Institute for International and Public Affairs]], [[Brown University]] |access-date=17 October 2024 |quote=In addition to killing people directly through traumatic injuries, wars cause "indirect deaths" by destroying, damaging, or causing deterioration of economic, social, psychological and health conditions. Most expansively, this report describes the causal pathways that can be expected to lead to far larger numbers of indirect deaths. These deaths result from diseases and other population-level health effects that stem from war’s destruction of public infrastructure and livelihood sources, reduced access to water and sanitation, environmental damage, and other such factors. This report builds on a foundation of previous Costs of War research for its framework and methodology in covering the most significant chains of impact, or causal pathways, to indirect war deaths in Gaza and the West Bank. Unlike in combat, these deaths do not necessarily occur immediately or in the close aftermath of the battles which many observers focus on. While it will take years to assess the full extent of these population-level health effects, they will inevitably lead to far higher numbers of deaths than direct violence.}}</ref><ref name="GazaHealthcareLettersEstimatedDeaths">{{cite web |url=https://static1.squarespace.com/static/66e083452b3cbf4bbd719aa2/t/66fcd754b472610b6335d66f/1727846228615/Appendix+20241002.pdf |title=Appendix to letter of October 2, 2024 re: American physicians observations from the Gaza Strip since October 7, 2023 |author=<!--Not stated--> |date=2 October 2024 |website=gazahealthcareletters.org |publisher=Gaza Healthcare Letters |access-date=17 October 2024 |quote=These are the most conservative estimates of the death toll that can be made with the given available data as of September 30, 2024. It is highly likely that the real number of deaths in Gaza from this conflict is far higher than this most conservative estimate. Without an immediate ceasefire the death toll will only continue to mount, especially among young children. |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250103061219/https://static1.squarespace.com/static/66e083452b3cbf4bbd719aa2/t/66fcd754b472610b6335d66f/1727846228615/Appendix+20241002.pdf |archive-date=3 January 2025}}</ref>

=== Water supply ===
{{See also|Water supply and sanitation in the State of Palestine|Targeting municipal services in Gaza}}
[[File:Humanitarian crisis in Gaza Strip following 2023 total blockade by Israel 1.png|thumb|Boy filling a water container with a [[garden hose]] in late-October 2023.]]
Before the war, Gaza purchased a small share of its water from Israel (6% in 2021).<ref>{{cite news |title=Gaza's limited water access, mapped |url=https://edition.cnn.com/2023/10/18/middleeast/gaza-water-access-supply-mapped-dg/index.html |access-date=27 October 2023 |work=[[CNN]] |date=18 October 2023 |archive-date=27 October 2023 pipelines exacerbated [[Water supply and sanitation in the State of Palestine|water supply issues in the Gaza Strip]], which already had a near lack of fit-to-drink [[aquifers]].<ref name="Akjsdfajkhasdkjfh" /> On 12 October, the United Nations said that Israeli actions had caused water shortages affecting 650,000 people.<ref name="ap8">{{cite news |date=12 October 2023 |title=Palestinians rush to buy food and struggle under strikes as Israel readies possible ground operation |work=[[Associated Press]] [[Doctors Without Borders]] stated on 18 December 2023 the water system in Gaza had collapsed.<ref>{{cite web |title=Inside Gaza: "Staying alive is only a matter of luck" |url=https://www.doctorswithoutborders.org/latest/inside-gaza-staying-alive-only-matter-luck |website=[[Doctors Without Borders]] |access-date=18 December 2023 |archive-date=18 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231218235716/https://www.doctorswithoutborders.org/latest/inside-gaza-staying-alive-only-matter-luck |url-status=live}}</ref> [[UNICEF]] reported children in southern Gaza were receiving 1.5 liters of water a day, while the minimum amount for survival is 3 liters per day.<ref>{{cite web |title='Barely a drop to drink': children in the Gaza Strip do not access 90 per cent of their normal water use |url=https://www.unicef.org/turkiye/en/press-releases/barely-drop-drink-children-gaza-strip-do-not-access-90-cent-their-normal-water-use#:~:text=AMMAN%2C%2020%20December%202023%20–%20Recently,survival%2C%20according%20to%20UNICEF%20estimates. |website=[[UNICEF]] |access-date=21 December 2023 |archive-date=21 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231221032922/https://www.unicef.org/turkiye/en/press-releases/barely-drop-drink-children-gaza-strip-do-not-access-90-cent-their-normal-water-use#:~:text=AMMAN%2C%2020%20December%202023%20–%20Recently,survival%2C%20according%20to%20UNICEF%20estimates. |url-status=live}}</ref> As of December 6, the sole water desalination facility in northern Gaza was inoperative, while the pipeline that delivers water from Israel to the north remained shut, thereby heightening the likelihood of dehydration and waterborne illnesses due to the consumption of unsafe water sources. IDF acknowledged it was flooding the tunnels on 30 January.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Kubovich |first1=Yaniv |title=Israeli Army Admits to Flooding Hamas Tunnels in Gaza in Bid to Destroy Them |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2024-01-30/ty-article/.premium/israeli-army-admits-to-flooding-hamas-tunnels-in-gaza-in-bid-to-destroy-them/0000018d-5b9e-d0af-a3af-7bbec4750000 |work=[[Haaretz]] |access-date=31 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240130191738/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2024-01-30/ty-article/.premium/israeli-army-admits-to-flooding-hamas-tunnels-in-gaza-in-bid-to-destroy-them/0000018d-5b9e-d0af-a3af-7bbec4750000 |archive-date=30 January 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Lawal |first1=Shola |date=3 February 2024 |title=How Israel's flooding of Gaza's tunnels will impact freshwater supply |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/features/2024/2/3/israel-floods-tunnels-with-seawater-what-impacts-on-gazas-water-supply |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=8 February 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240228145957/https://www.aljazeera.com/features/2024/2/3/israel-floods-tunnels-with-seawater-what-impacts-on-gazas-water-supply |archive-date=28 February 2024}}</ref>

In January 2024, the Israeli army destroyed Gaza City’s main reservoirs, Al-Balad and Al-Rimal.<ref>{{cite news |title=Lack of access to clean drinking water is a death sentence for the people of Gaza |url=https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/lack-access-clean-drinking-water-death-sentence-people-gaza-enar |work=[[ReliefWeb]] |date=15 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240301131537/https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/lack-access-clean-drinking-water-death-sentence-people-gaza-enar |archive-date=1 March 2024}}</ref> The director of ambulance and emergency centres for Gaza stated on 20 January that the "struggle for water is a daily torment".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Muzaffar |first1=Maroosha |title=Biden says Israel not opposed to two-state solution for Palestinians |url=https://au.news.yahoo.com/biden-says-israel-not-opposed-092034683.html |work=[[Yahoo! News]] |date=20 January 2024 |agency=[[The Independent]] |access-date=22 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240219080903/https://au.news.yahoo.com/biden-says-israel-not-opposed-092034683.html |archive-date=19 February 2024}}</ref> The UNOCHA director for Gaza stated, "We can only meet a third of the population’s need for clean drinking water."<ref>{{cite news |title=2.2 million at risk of starvation in Gaza |url=https://www.newarab.com/news/israel-escalates-attack-gaza-despite-icj-genocide-ruling |work=[[The New Arab]] |date=27 January 2024 |access-date=31 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240131075253/https://www.newarab.com/news/israel-escalates-attack-gaza-despite-icj-genocide-ruling |archive-date=31 January 2024}}</ref>

In February 2024, the [[Food and Agriculture Organization]] stated water was at 7 percent of pre-October levels.<ref>{{cite web |last1=Martina |first1=Maurizio |title=Gaza: In a briefing to the UN Security Council, FAO calls for immediate cessation of hostilities and restoration of humanitarian space to eliminate the risk of famine |url=https://www.un.org/unispal/document/gaza-in-a-briefing-to-the-un-security-council-fao-27feb2024/ |website=[[United Nations]] |access-date=29 February 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240301132317/https://www.un.org/unispal/document/gaza-in-a-briefing-to-the-un-security-council-fao-27feb2024/ |archive-date=1 March 2024}}</ref> In May 2024, the [[Coastal Municipalities Water Utility]] reported, "The entire water supply and sewage management systems are nearing total collapse because the damage is so extensive".<ref>{{cite web |last1=Zhang |first1=Sharon |title=Oxfam Report: Conditions "Ripe" for Cholera, Hepatitis A Outbreak in Gaza |url=https://truthout.org/articles/oxfam-report-conditions-ripe-for-cholera-hepatitis-a-outbreak-in-gaza/ |website=[[truthout]] |date=13 May 2024 |access-date=20 May 2024 |archive-date=20 May 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240520002432/https://truthout.org/articles/oxfam-report-conditions-ripe-for-cholera-hepatitis-a-outbreak-in-gaza/ |url-status=live}}</ref> UNOCHA stated some displaced people were surviving on 3 percent of minimum daily water needs.<ref>{{cite web |title=Hostilities in the Gaza Strip and Israel Flash Update #170 |url=https://www.ochaopt.org/content/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-170 |website=[[OCHA]] |date=24 May 2024 |publisher=[[United Nations]] |access-date=4 June 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240604032101/https://www.ochaopt.org/content/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-170 |archive-date=4 June 2024}}</ref> UNICEF made a deal with Israel in June 2024 to restore a desalination plant.<ref>{{cite news |title=UNICEF Says Deal Agreed With Israel To Boost Gaza Water Supply |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/unicef-says-deal-agreed-with-israel-to-boost-gaza-water-supply-b45e5e3b# |work=[[Barron's]] |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]] |access-date=6 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240804131532/https://www.barrons.com/news/unicef-says-deal-agreed-with-israel-to-boost-gaza-water-supply-b45e5e3b |archive-date=4 August 2024}}</ref>

In July 2024, the Israeli military stated it had allowed power to be restored to a desalination plant in Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Rabinovitch |first1=Ari |title=Israel connects power line to Gaza plant to boost drinking water supply |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israel-connects-power-line-gaza-plant-boost-drinking-water-supply-2024-07-02/ |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=13 July 2024}}</ref> Children in Al-Mawasi were waiting six to eight hours a day looking for water, with officials stating facilities serving as many as 700,000 people were out of service.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Da Silva |first1=Chantal |title=Clean water becomes an increasingly scarce resource in Gaza amid Israeli offensive |url=https://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/israel-hamas-war-gaza-water-scarce-dehydration-warnings-unrwa-rcna162257 |work=[[NBC News]] |date=18 July 2024 |access-date=23 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240808070218/https://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/israel-hamas-war-gaza-water-scarce-dehydration-warnings-unrwa-rcna162257 |archive-date=8 August 2024}}</ref> By August 2024, UNRWA warned that Gaza's water crisis had grown more severe, with people only receiving about half of the required liters of water per day.<ref>{{cite news |title=Gaza's water crisis catastrophic amid ongoing war and severe shortages |url=https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HGPmJD5-JC8 |via=[[YouTube]] |date=18 August 2024 |work=[[Al Jazeera English]] |access-date=12 September 2024}}</ref> Children were reported to be drinking from puddles due to the lack of available drinking water.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Stockwell |first1=Billy |last2=Haq |first2=Sana Noor |title=Children are drinking from puddles and wading through sewage pools, as Israel pummels water systems in Gaza |url=https://www.cnn.com/2024/08/23/middleeast/israel-gaza-water-shortages-heatwave-crisis-intl/index.html |work=[[CNN]] |date=23 August 2024 |access-date=12 September 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241220164226/https://www.cnn.com/2024/08/23/middleeast/israel-gaza-water-shortages-heatwave-crisis-intl/index.html |archive-date=20 December 2024}}</ref>

== Disease ==
=== Physical health and disease ===
{{See also|2024 Gaza Strip polio epidemic}}{{Tweet
| name = World Health Organization
| username = WHO
| text = As deaths and injuries in Gaza continue to rise due to intensified hostilities, intense overcrowding and disrupted health, water, and sanitation systems pose an added danger: the rapid spread of infectious diseases.
| date = November 8, 2023
| reference = <ref>{{cite web |title=Risk of disease spread soars in #Gaza as health facilities, water and sanitation systems disrupted |url=https://twitter.com/WHO/status/1722310494155866430 |website=X |publisher=[[World Health Organization]] |access-date=10 November 2023 |archive-date=10 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231110040437/https://twitter.com/WHO/status/1722310494155866430 |url-status=live}}</ref>
| ID = 1722310494155866430
| image = Logo du CCOMS.jpg
| width = 230px
}}

Public health experts warned of the outbreak and spread of disease in Gaza. According to [[Oxfam]] and the United Nations, Gaza's lack of clean water and [[Waste management|sanitation]] would trigger a rise in [[cholera]] and other deadly [[Infection|infectious diseases]].<ref name="Gaza’s next big threat">{{cite news |last1=Marsi |first1=Federica |title=Gaza's next big threat: Cholera, infectious diseases amid Israeli blockade |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/21/gazas-next-big-threat-cholera-infectious-diseases-amid-total-blockade |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=24 October 2023 |archive-date=21 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231021023934/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/21/gazas-next-big-threat-cholera-infectious-diseases-amid-total-blockade |url-status=live}}</ref> Oxfam stated Gaza's [[Sewage treatment|sewage pumping stations]] and [[wastewater treatment]] facilities had ceased operations, so the buildup of solid waste and [[Health risks from dead bodies|unburied bodies]] were likely vectors of disease.<ref name="Gaza’s next big threat" /> Due to the lack of [[Drinking water|clean drinking water]], Gaza residents were drinking water contaminated with [[sewage]], [[seawater]], and [[farm water]], another major source of disease.<ref name="Gaza’s next big threat" /> Richard Brennan, regional emergency director at [[World Health Organization|WHO]], stated, "The conditions are ripe for the spread of a number of diarrhoeal and skin diseases".<ref name="Gaza’s next big threat" />

Doctors also warned of overcrowded conditions at schools and hospitals. Dr. Nahed Abu Taaema stated overcrowded shelters were "a prime breeding ground for disease to spread".<ref name="Overcrowding, poor sanitation">{{cite news |first1=Joseph |last1=Stepansky |first2=Farah |last2=Najjar |first3=Arwa |last3=Ibrahim |date=23 October 2023 |title=Overcrowding, poor sanitation breeding disease in Gaza: Doctors |url=https://aje.io/j9jahf?update=2434322 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=24 October 2023 |archive-date=26 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231026024932/https://aje.io/j9jahf?update=2434322 |url-status=live}}</ref> Abu Taaema reported a rise in rashes, lung infections, and stomach issues.<ref name="Overcrowding, poor sanitation" /> On 24 October, the [[Gaza Health Ministry]] recorded 3,150 cases of disease from drinking [[Water pollution|contaminated water]], mostly among children.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Yazbek |first1=Hiba |title=Israel-Hamas War U.N. Secretary General Calls for Cease-Fire as Israel Intensifies Airstrikes |work=[[The New York Times]] |date=24 October 2023 |url=https://www.nytimes.com/live/2023/10/24/world/israel-hamas-war-gaza-news/a9ae6351-0219-5682-9bcb-68fb81481490?smid=url-share |access-date=24 October 2023 |archive-date=26 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231026024930/https://www.nytimes.com/live/2023/10/24/world/israel-hamas-war-gaza-news/a9ae6351-0219-5682-9bcb-68fb81481490?smid=url-share |url-status=live}}</ref> The lack of [[medical supplies]] was another reported issue, as the World Health Organization reported a sanitation crisis in hospitals, with some struggling to sanitize [[Surgical instrument|surgical equipment]].<ref>{{cite news |last1=Paddison |first1=Laura |last2=Marsh |first2=Rene |title=Gazans forced to drink dirty, salty water as the fuel needed to run water systems runs out |url=https://www.cnn.com/2023/10/24/middleeast/gaza-water-war-climate-intl-cmd/index.html |work=[[CNN]] |date=24 October 2023 |access-date=25 October 2023 |archive-date=25 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231025014559/https://www.cnn.com/2023/10/24/middleeast/gaza-water-war-climate-intl-cmd/index.html |url-status=live}}</ref> Dr. Iyad Issa Abu Zaher stated, "The outbreak of disease is inevitable".<ref name="Gaza kidney">{{cite news |last1=Alsaafin |first1=Linah |last2=Amra |first2=Ashraf |title='Terrifying': Gaza kidney patients face dialysis crisis at packed hospitals |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/features/2023/10/25/terrifying-hope-shrinks-for-gazas-dialysis-patients-at-packed-hospitals |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=25 October 2023 |archive-date=25 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231025031525/https://www.aljazeera.com/features/2023/10/25/terrifying-hope-shrinks-for-gazas-dialysis-patients-at-packed-hospitals |url-status=live}}</ref> UNRWA schools, where an estimated 600,000 Gazans were sheltering, reported outbreaks of [[scabies]] and [[chicken pox]], as well as a lack of basic hygiene for women [[Menstrual cycle|menstruating]].<ref>{{cite news |last1=Mousa |first1=Aseel |title=Displaced Palestinians in overcrowded UN schools face outbreak of disease |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/27/displaced-palestinians-in-overcrowded-un-schools-face-outbreak-of-disease |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=27 October 2023 |archive-date=27 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231027120502/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/27/displaced-palestinians-in-overcrowded-un-schools-face-outbreak-of-disease |url-status=live}}</ref> On 27 October, [[Action Against Hunger]] warned people were developing [[kidney failure]] due to the consumption of [[salinity|salt water]] and [[dehydration]].<ref name="AAH-Oct27">{{cite news |last=Cullinan |first=Meril |date=27 October 2023 |title=Gaza: Water and Sanitation Crisis Grows |website=Action Against Hunger |language=en-US |url=https://www.actionagainsthunger.org/press-releases/gaza-water-and-sanitation-crisis-grows/ |access-date=2 November 2023 |archive-date=2 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231102201818/https://www.actionagainsthunger.org/press-releases/gaza-water-and-sanitation-crisis-grows/ |url-status=live}}</ref>

On 6 November, [[OCHA]] stated [[Disability|individuals with disabilities]] were suffering disproportionately due to the lack of accommodations in most shelters.<ref>{{cite news |first=Joseph |last=Stepansky |date=6 November 2023 |title=Disabled in Gaza suffering disproportionate harm, aid groups warn |url=https://aje.io/91bdr3?update=2466477 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=6 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231121104157/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/11/6/israel-hamas-live-news-communications-blackout-across-gaza?update=2466477 |archive-date=21 November 2023}}</ref> UNRWA announced cases of respiratory infections, diarrhoea and chicken pox had been reported at its shelters.<ref>{{cite news |first=Joseph |last=Stepansky |date=6 November 2023 |title=Diseases reported in crowded Gaza shelters |url=https://aje.io/91bdr3?update=2466385 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=6 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231215223755/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/11/6/israel-hamas-live-news-communications-blackout-across-gaza?update=2466385 |archive-date=15 December 2023}}</ref> On 10 November, WHO stated infectious diseases, including diarrhea and chickenpox, were soaring across the Gaza Strip.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Lodhi |first1=Areesha |title=How bad is Gaza's disease outbreak amid the Israel war? |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/11/10/how-bad-is-gazas-disease-outbreak-amid-the-israel-war |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=10 November 2023 |archive-date=10 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231110111932/http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/11/10/how-bad-is-gazas-disease-outbreak-amid-the-israel-war |url-status=live}}</ref> OCHA stated [[waste management|accumulated waste]] in the streets risked the spread of airborne diseases and infestations of [[insect]]s and [[rat]]s.<ref>{{cite news |first1=Usaid |last1=Siddiqui |first2=Virginia |last2=Pietromarchi |date=11 November 2023 |title=Accumulation of waste leading to insect infestation: UN |url=https://aje.io/jmh2l8?update=2479805 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=11 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231121140614/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/11/11/israel-hamas-war-live-pleas-for-help-as-israel-bombards-gaza-hospitals?update=2479805 |archive-date=21 November 2023}}</ref> Doctors reported that due to a lack of fresh water and [[iodine]], patients wounds were often infested with [[maggot]]s.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Harouda |first1=Ameera |last2=Abi-Habib |first2=Maria |last3=Abu Bakr |first3=Bashir |title=As Gaza Hospitals Collapse, Medical Workers Face the Hardest Choices |work=[[The New York Times]] |date=6 November 2023 |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/11/06/world/middleeast/gaza-hospitals-israel-war.html |access-date=12 November 2023 |archive-date=11 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231111201344/https://www.nytimes.com/2023/11/06/world/middleeast/gaza-hospitals-israel-war.html |url-status=live}}</ref>

Raw sewage overflowed in the streets, creating a health and [[environmental disaster]].<ref>{{cite news |title=Sewage Is Flowing into the Streets because Pumps Don't Have Electricity |date=13 November 2023 |url=https://calgaryherald.com/news/israel-middle-east-israel-hamas-war-day-38 |work=[[Calgary Herald]] |agency=[[Associated Press]] |access-date=14 November 2023 |archive-date=18 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231118052853/https://calgaryherald.com/news/israel-middle-east-israel-hamas-war-day-38 |url-status=live}}</ref> On 8 November, the World Health Organization stated that since the start of the conflict, 33,551 cases of diarrhea had been reported, 8,944 cases of [[scabies]] and [[lice]], 1,005 cases of chickenpox, 12,635 cases of [[skin rash]] and 54,866 cases of [[upper respiratory infection]]s.<ref>{{cite web |title=Risk of disease spread soars in Gaza as health facilities, water and sanitation systems disrupted |url=https://www.emro.who.int/media/news/risk-of-disease-spread-soars-in-gaza-as-health-facilities-water-and-sanitation-systems-disrupted.html |website=[[World Health Organization]] |access-date=15 November 2023 |archive-date=15 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231115035156/https://www.emro.who.int/media/news/risk-of-disease-spread-soars-in-gaza-as-health-facilities-water-and-sanitation-systems-disrupted.html |url-status=live}}</ref> On 17 November, WHO updated these numbers, stating there were 70,000 cases of acute respiratory infections and over 44,000 cases of diarrhea, which were significantly higher than expected.<ref>{{cite news |title=WHO voices concern over spread of disease in Gaza |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/who-voices-concern-over-spread-disease-gaza-2023-11-17/ |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=17 November 2023 |archive-date=17 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231117110354/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/who-voices-concern-over-spread-disease-gaza-2023-11-17/ |url-status=live}}</ref> [[UNICEF]] warned the worsening sanitation situation threatened a mass disease outbreak.<ref>{{cite news |title=Gaza Sanitation 'Perfect Storm For Tragedy': UN |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/gaza-sanitation-perfect-storm-for-tragedy-un-01c8acfe |magazine=[[Barron's]] |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]] |access-date=21 November 2023 On 28 November, WHO stated more Palestinians risked dying from disease than bombings.<ref>{{cite news |title=More Palestinians at risk of death from disease than bombings: WHO's warning |url=https://www.hindustantimes.com/world-news/more-palestinians-at-risk-of-death-from-disease-than-bombings-whos-warning-101701167334463.html |work=[[The Hindustan Times]] |date=28 November 2023 |archive-date=4 December 2023}}</ref> UNRWA chief [[Philippe Lazzarini]] warned of an impending humanitarian "tsunami" as people succumbed to disease and the deprivation of sanitation and clean water.<ref>{{cite news |last1=England |first1=Andrew |title=UN warns of humanitarian 'tsunami' as Israel-Hamas hostilities resume |url-status=live}}</ref> On 7 December, the World Health Organization reported increases in acute respiratory infections, scabies, [[jaundice]], and diarrhea.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Harb |first1=Hajar March 2024}}</ref> On 13 December, 360,000 cases of infectious diseases were reported in shelters.<ref>{{cite web |title=Hostilities in the Gaza Strip and Israel |url=https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-67 |website=[[ReliefWeb]] |date=13 December 2023 |publisher=[[UNOCHA]] |access-date=13 March 2024}}</ref> On 20 December, WHO reported Gaza was experiencing "soaring rates of infectious disease outbreaks".<ref>{{cite web |title=Hostilities in the Gaza Strip and Israel |url=https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-74 |website=[[ReliefWeb]] |date=20 December 2023 |publisher=[[OCHA]] |access-date=21 |archive-date=1 March 2024}}</ref>

On 29 December, WHO chief Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus reported 180,000 cases of upper respiratory infections, 136,400 cases of diarrhoea, 55,400 cases of lice and scabies, 5,330 cases of chickenpox, 42,700 cases of skin rash, and 4,722 cases of [[impetigo]].<ref>{{cite news |title=WHO Chief 'Very Concerned' By Gaza Infectious Disease Threat |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/who-chief-very-concerned-by-gaza-infectious-disease-threat-1200fd63 |magazine=[[Barron's]] |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]] |access-date=30 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231230001647/https://www.barrons.com/news/who-chief-very-concerned-by-gaza-infectious-disease-threat-1200fd63 |archive-date=30 December 2023}}</ref> Flooding in Gaza spread sewage water, raising fears of the spread of disease.<ref>{{cite web |title=Gaza flooding latest disaster to hit desperate Palestinians |url=https://news.un.org/en/story/2023/12/1144802#:~:text=Water%20and%20sanitation%20emergency,compounding%20risks%20of%20disease%20spread. |website=UN News |date=14 December 2023 |publisher=[[United Nations]] |access-date=7 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240118020926/https://news.un.org/en/story/2023/12/1144802 |archive-date=18 January 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |first1=Linah |last1=Alsaafin |first2=Brian |last2=Osgood |date=6 January 2024 |title=Gaza's Jabalia refugee camp overrun with sewage water |archive-date=7 January 2024}}</ref> On 19 January, [[Yahya Al-Sarraj]], the mayor of [[Gaza City]], stated more than 50,000 tons of trash had accumulated in the city, further leading to the spread of disease.<ref>{{cite news |first=Brian |last=Osgood |date=19 January 2024 |title=Gaza City mayor: Fuel depletion poses challenge to providing services |archive-date=19 February 2024}}</ref> Parents reported children falling sick after being exposed to raw sewage.<ref>{{cite news |title=WHO: three in four Palestinians in Gaza internally displaced |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2024/jan/20/middle-east-crisis-live-biden-two-state-solution-netanyahu-israel-gaza-hamas?filterKeyEvents=false&page=with:block-65ac0d948f082472faf43c4f |work=[[The Guardian]] |date=21 January 2024 |access-date=22 January 2024 |last1=Yang |first1=Maya |last2=Sedghi |first2=Amy |last3=Abdul |first3=Geneva |last4=Fulton |first4=Adam |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240219080902/https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2024/jan/20/middle-east-crisis-live-biden-two-state-solution-netanyahu-israel-gaza-hamas?filterKeyEvents=false&page=with:block-65ac0d948f082472faf43c4f |archive-date=19 February 2024}}</ref>

In his address to the UN Security Council on 31 January 2024, Martin Griffiths, the UN under-secretary general for humanitarian affairs and emergency relief coordination, provided a comprehensive overview of the challenges currently confronting numerous individuals in Gaza. According to our latest estimates, approximately 75 percent of the entire population has been displaced. The living conditions they endure are deplorable and deteriorating with each passing day. The makeshift tent camps, established by refugees and displaced people, are being inundated by heavy rains, compelling children, parents, and the elderly to seek shelter in the mud. The issue of food insecurity continues to escalate, while access to clean water remains almost entirely unattainable. Given the limited availability of public health support, preventable diseases are rampant and will persistently propagate.<ref name="Humanitarian impact of the conflict"/> On 4 March, the Gaza Health Ministry stated they had recorded about one million cases of infectious diseases.<ref>{{cite news |first1=Usaid |last1=Siddiqui |first2=Maziar |last2=Motamedi |date=4 March 2024 |title=Gaza Health Ministry: We detected about one million cases of infectious diseases |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/3/4/israels-war-on-gaza-live-israel-repeats-attacks-as-children-die-of-hunger?update=2747606 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=6 March 2024 |archive-date=4 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240304192046/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/3/4/israels-war-on-gaza-live-israel-repeats-attacks-as-children-die-of-hunger?update=2747606 |url-status=live}}</ref>

The situation in Gaza is worsening, leading to the spread of diseases due to the lack of clean water and insufficient sewage facilities. According to the United Nations, the people in Gaza are facing a shortage of water and hygiene materials, which is negatively impacting their overall well-being and physical health. Additionally, the accumulation of solid waste in public areas, hospitals, IDP shelters, and other locations is a major concern as it poses significant risks to public health. The uncollected waste, amounting to tens of thousands of tons, is exacerbating these risks.<ref name="Humanitarian impact of the conflict"/> In April 2024, the Gaza Media Office stated environmental contamination in northern Gaza had reached "unprecedented levels" due to "mountains of waste and hundreds of mass graves".<ref>{{cite news |first1=Nils |last1=Adler |first2=Farah |last2=Najjar |date=15 April 2024 |title=Northern Gaza faces 'unprecedented levels' of contamination, media office says |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/4/15/israels-war-on-gaza-live-five-killed-in-nuseirat-as-israel-strikes-camps?update=2838858 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=17 April 2024 |archive-date=17 April 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240417035546/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/4/15/israels-war-on-gaza-live-five-killed-in-nuseirat-as-israel-strikes-camps?update=2838858 |url-status=live}}</ref> In May 2024, the UN stated, "Mosquitoes, flies and rats are spreading, and so are diseases."<ref>{{cite news |first1=Maziar |last1=Motamedi |first2=Usaid |last2=Siddiqui |date=5 May 2024 |title=UN sounds alarms on 'sanitation crisis' in war-stricken Gaza |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/5/5/israels-war-on-gaza-live-neither-side-willing-to-budge-in-truce-talks?update=2880934 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=10 May |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240510033627/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/5/5/israels-war-on-gaza-live-neither-side-willing-to-budge-in-truce-talks?update=2880934 |url-status=live}}</ref> Oxfam reported the threat of disease outbreaks due to an accumulation of "human waste and rivers of sewage in the streets".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Shurafa |first1=Wafaa |title=Misery deepens in Gaza's Rafah as Israeli troops press operation |url=https://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/misery-deepens-gazas-rafah-israeli-troops-press-operation-110173165 |work=[[ABC News (United States)|ABC News]] |agency=[[Associated Press]] |access-date=20 May 2024 |archive-date=20 May 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240520002613/https://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/misery-deepens-gazas-rafah-israeli-troops-press-operation-110173165 |url-status=live}}</ref>

In July 2024, [[poliovirus]] was detected in Gaza's sewage water.<ref>{{cite news |date=19 July 2024 |title=Highly infectious poliovirus found in Gaza sewage samples |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/article/2024/jul/19/israel-gaza-war-polio-sewage-samples |work=[[The Guardian]] |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]] |access-date=27 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240802100006/https://www.theguardian.com/world/article/2024/jul/19/israel-gaza-war-polio-sewage-samples |archive-date=2 August 2024}}</ref> On 29 July, The Gaza Health Ministry officially declared a [[2024 Gaza Strip polio epidemic|polio epidemic in the Gaza Strip]].<ref name=":32">{{Cite news |last= |first= |date=30 July 2024 |title=Gaza Health Ministry Declares Territory 'Polio Epidemic Area' |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/gaza-health-ministry-declares-territory-polio-epidemic-area-24da98d1 |access-date=30 July 2024 |work=[[Barron's]] |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]] |language=en-US |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240730191947/https://www.barrons.com/news/gaza-health-ministry-declares-territory-polio-epidemic-area-24da98d1 |archive-date=30 July 2024}}</ref>

According to a letter sent to President [[Joseph R. Biden]], Vice President [[Kamala D. Harris]], and others on October 2, 2024 by 99 American healthcare workers who have served in the Gaza Strip since October 7, 2023, and cited in a study from the [[Watson Institute for International and Public Affairs]] at [[Brown University]], at least 5,000 people in Gaza have died due to a lack of access to care for chronic diseases according to a conservative estimate.<ref name="MotherJonesTotalDeaths" /><ref name="WatsonInstituteEstimatedDeaths" /><ref name="GazaHealthcareLettersEstimatedDeaths" />

=== Psychological health ===
{{See also|Mental health in Palestine}}
Weeks of continuous air strikes and explosions have contributed to the psychological destruction of children in Gaza. Following 16 days of bombardment, children developed severe trauma, with symptoms including convulsion, aggression, bed-wetting, and nervousness. 90% of children in pediatric hospitals in Gaza exhibited or reported symptoms of anxiety, the majority exhibited post-traumatic stress symptoms, and 82% reported fears of imminent death.<ref>{{Cite news |date=18 July 2024 |title=Bedwetting, nightmares and shaking. War in Gaza takes a mental health toll, especially on children |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-gaza-war-children-mental-health-370c7ccc24dcc8a2c4b81acd5345221b |access-date=19 July |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240724233719/https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-gaza-war-children-mental-health-370c7ccc24dcc8a2c4b81acd5345221b |archive-date=24 July 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/oct/22/children-in-gaza-developing-severe-trauma-after-16-days-of-bombing#:~:text=Children%20had%20“started%20to%20develop,most%20impacted%2C”%20he%20said. |title=Children in Gaza 'developing severe trauma' after 16 days of bombing |date=15 October 2023 |work=[[The Guardian]] |access-date=10 November 2023 |archive-date=22 October 2023 == Healthcare ==
{{main|Attacks on health facilities during the Gaza war}}
{{See also|Health in the State of Palestine|Timeline of the Gaza Strip healthcare collapse}}
[[File:Damage in Gaza Strip during the October 2023 - 42 (cropped).jpg|thumb|Doctor with wounded child, [[Al-Shifa hospital|Al-Shifa]].]]

The [[Healthcare in the State of Palestine|healthcare system of Gaza]] faced several humanitarian crises as a result of the conflict. Due to Israel's siege, hospitals faced a lack of fuel and relied on [[backup generator]]s for the first two weeks of the war.<ref>{{cite magazine |last1=Browne |first1=Grace |title='The whole health system is collapsing around us.' hospitals began shutting down as they ran out of fuel, starting with the [[Indonesia Hospital]].<ref>{{cite news |title=Gaza hospital generators to run out of fuel in 48 hours: Health Ministry By 5 January 2024, the World Health Organization reported there had been 304 attacks on healthcare facilities in Gaza since 7 October, with 606 deaths.<ref>{{cite web |title=Nearly 600 attacks on healthcare in Gaza and West Bank since war began: WHO |url=https://news.un.org/en/story/2024/01/1145317 |website=UN News |date=5 January 2024 |publisher=[[United Nations]] |access-date=5 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240229232402/https://news.un.org/en/story/2024/01/1145317 |archive-date=29 February 2024}}</ref> On 24 January, WHO stated seven out of 24 hospitals remained partially operational in Northern Gaza, and seven out of 12 in Southern Gaza.<ref>{{cite web |title=WHO and partners bring fuel to Al-Shifa, as remaining hospitals in Gaza face growing threats |url=https://www.who.int/news/item/24-01-2024-who-and-partners-bring-fuel-to-al-shifa--as-remaining-hospitals-in-gaza-face-growing-threats#:~:text=Seven%20out%20of%2024%20hospitals,food%20for%20patients%20or%20staff. |website=[[World Health Organization]] |access-date=25 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240229185127/https://www.who.int/news/item/24-01-2024-who-and-partners-bring-fuel-to-al-shifa--as-remaining-hospitals-in-gaza-face-growing-threats |archive-date=29 February 2024}}</ref> On 26 January, a senior [[OHCHR]] official stated, "I fear that many more civilians will die. The continued attacks on specially protected facilities, such as hospitals, will kill civilians".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Tétrault-Farber |first1=Gabrielle |date=26 January 2024 |title=Deadly attacks on Gaza, cold weather making it 'uninhabitable' - U.N. |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/deadly-attacks-gaza-cold-weather-making-it-uninhabitable-un-2024-01-26/ |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=27 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240623084043/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/deadly-attacks-gaza-cold-weather-making-it-uninhabitable-un-2024-01-26/ |archive-date=23 June 2024}}</ref> The same day, a [[Doctors Without Borders]] coordinator stated, "There is no longer a healthcare system in Gaza."<ref>{{cite web |title=With Nasser hospital out of commission, people in southern Gaza run out of healthcare options |url=https://www.msf.org/nasser-hospital-out-commission-people-southern-gaza-run-out-healthcare-options |website=[[Doctors Without Borders]] |access-date=31 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240207105902/https://www.msf.org/nasser-hospital-out-commission-people-southern-gaza-run-out-healthcare-options |archive-date=7 February 2024}}</ref> A senior technical adviser with the [[International Rescue Committee]] stated, "There’s nothing that could have prepared me for the horrors that I saw."<ref>{{cite magazine |last1=Chotiner |first1=Isaac |author1-link=Isaac Chotiner |title=A Pediatrician's Two Weeks Inside a Hospital in Gaza |url=https://www.newyorker.com/news/q-and-a/a-pediatricians-two-weeks-inside-a-hospital-in-gaza |magazine=[[The New Yorker]] |date=30 January 2024 |access-date=31 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240301011042/https://www.newyorker.com/news/q-and-a/a-pediatricians-two-weeks-inside-a-hospital-in-gaza |archive-date=1 March 2024}}</ref> In May 2024, the [[UN Development Programme]] stated the conflict could reduce levels of health back to 1980 levels.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Burke |first1=Jason |title=Rebuilding homes in Gaza will cost $40bn and take 16 years, UN finds |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/article/2024/may/02/rebuilding-homes-in-gaza-will-cost-40bn-and-take-16-years-un-finds |website=The Guardian |date=2 May 2024 |access-date=7 May 2024}}</ref>

=== Supplies shortages ===
Following the [[Gaza electricity crisis|shutdown of the Gaza Strip power station]] on 11 October, it was reported that hospitals in Gaza would soon run out of available fuel to power generators.<ref>{{cite news |last=Cormack |first=Lucy |date=12 October 2023 |url=https://www.smh.com.au/world/middle-east/the-gaza-hospitals-with-just-three-days-of-generator-power-left-20231011-p5ebkq.html |title=The Gaza hospitals with just three days of generator power left |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231017110145/https://www.smh.com.au/world/middle-east/the-gaza-hospitals-with-just-three-days-of-generator-power-left-20231011-p5ebkq.html |archive-date=17 October 2023 |work=[[The Sydney Morning Herald]]}}</ref> The Al-Aqsa Martyrs Hospital faced a [[Kidney dialysis|dialysis]] crisis, with hundreds sharing only 24 dialysis machines.<ref name="Gaza kidney" /> WHO announced it could no longer resupply al-Shifa and al-Quds hospitals due to the high levels of risk.<ref>{{cite news |title=WHO unable to resupply Shifa and al-Quds hospitals, says official |url=https://aje.io/py7et7?update=2449481 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=30 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240303121423/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/10/30/israel-hamas-war-live-palestinian-death-toll-gaza-rises-above-8000?update=2449481 |archive-date=3 March 2024}}</ref> In November, nearly half of all hospitals were out of service due to shortages of fuel and power, and [[amputation]]s and [[caesarean section|C-sections]] were performed without anesthetic due to shortages of supplies.<ref name="auto14">{{Cite news |last=Andrew |first=Sadie |date=5 November 2023 |title=In Gaza, being a mother is a matter of life and death |url=https://www.cnn.com/2023/11/05/middleeast/israel-strikes-gaza-women-children-health-crisis-mime-intl/index.html |access-date=8 November 2023 |work=[[CNN]] |language=en |archive-date=8 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231108032839/https://www.cnn.com/2023/11/05/middleeast/israel-strikes-gaza-women-children-health-crisis-mime-intl/index.html |url-status=live}}</ref>

On 8 November, Al-Quds completely ran out of fuel and shut down most services.<ref>{{cite news |title=Al-Quds Hospital in Gaza runs out of fuel, shuts down key services |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/11/8/al-quds-hospital-in-gaza-runs-out-of-fuel-shuts-down-key-services |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=11 November 2023 |archive-date=11 |url-status=live}}</ref> On 13 November, Kamal Adwan Hospital ran out of fuel.<ref>{{cite news |title=Kamal Adwan Hospital has run out of fuel – report |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2023/nov/12/israel-hamas-war-live-netanyahu-vows-to-press-on-with-full-force-as-fighting-rages-around-main-gaza-hospital?filterKeyEvents=false&page=with:block-655175d98f08c3ba45a520bc#block-655175d98f08c3ba45a520bc |url-status=live |last1=Sullivan |first1=Helen |last2=Yang |first2=Maya |last3=Belam |first3=Martin |last4=Kearney |first4=Christine}}</ref> The al-Amal Hospital's only generator shut down.<ref>{{cite news |title=The Palestine Red Crescent Society (PRCS) has said that the only power generator at Al-Amal hospital in southern Gaza has stopped working. |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2023/nov/13/israel-hamas-war-live-updates-al-shifa-hospital-who-us-strikes-syria-palestine |work=[[The Guardian]] |access-date=13 November 2023 On 6 December, Doctors Without Borders stated fuel and medical supplies at al-Aqsa hospital were critically low.<ref>{{cite news |title=Fuel and medical supplies running out at al-Aqsa hospital in central Gaza, Doctors Without Borders says |archive-date=19 December 2023}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2023/dec/07/israel-hamas-war-live-updates-hamas-leader-hiding-underground-idf-says-gaza-aid-system-collapse-news-palestine |title=Israel-Hamas war live: Gaza aid system at 'severe risk of collapse', says UN secretary-general |work=[[The Guardian]] |date=8 December 2023 |last1=Ahmad |first1=Reged |last2=Chao-Fong |first2=Léonie |last3=Luscombe |first3=Richard |last4=Hall |first4=Rachel |last5=Abdul |first5=Geneva |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240225225228/https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2023/dec/07/israel-hamas-war-live-updates-hamas-leader-hiding-underground-idf-says-gaza-aid-system-collapse-news-palestine |archive-date=25 February 2024}}</ref> Doctors at [[Nasser Medical Complex]] in [[Khan Younis]] described a lack of supplies and barely any medical functionality.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Babas |first1=Ana |title=At 1 Gaza hospital, doctors are fleeing, supplies are low and there are not enough beds |url=https://www.npr.org/2023/12/12/1218692478/gaza-hospital-israel-hamas-khan-younis |work=[[NPR]] |access-date=13 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240128002811/https://www.npr.org/2023/12/12/1218692478/gaza-hospital-israel-hamas-khan-younis |archive-date=28 January 2024}}</ref>

From 11 October 2023 onwards, the Gaza Strip has experienced a complete lack of electricity due to the Israeli authorities discontinuing the power supply and depleting the fuel reserves for Gaza's only power plant. The United Nations has observed that this ongoing blackout, along with the shutdown of communications and industrial fuel, is greatly impeding the aid community's ability to assess and effectively address the worsening humanitarian crisis.<ref name="Humanitarian impact of the conflict">{{cite web |url=https://lordslibrary.parliament.uk/humanitarian-situation-in-gaza/ |title=Humanitarian impact of the conflict |website=[[House of Commons Library]] |date=5 February 2024 |access-date=13 February 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240214200919/https://lordslibrary.parliament.uk/humanitarian-situation-in-gaza/ |archive-date=14 February 2024 |last1=Tobin |first1=James}}</ref>

On 14 October, the Diagnostic Cancer Treatment Centre of the [[Al-Ahli Arab Hospital]] was partially destroyed by Israeli rocket fire.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.anglicannews.org/news/2023/10/anglican-run-al-ahli-arab-hospital-in-gaza-damaged-by-israeli-rocket-fire-as-conflict-continues.aspx |title=Anglican-run al-Ahli Arab Hospital in Gaza |archive-date=19 October 2023 |work=Anglican Communion News Service |access-date=17 October 2023}}</ref> In a statement on 15 October, the [[World Health Organization]] stated four hospitals were no longer functioning after being targeted by Israeli airstrikes.<ref>{{cite news |last=Sforza |first=Lauren |date=16 October 2023 On 30 October, the [[Turkish-Palestinian Friendship Hospital]] was severely damaged by an Israeli airstrike.<ref>{{cite news |title=Turkish-Palestinian Friendship Hospital in Gaza severely damaged from Israeli airstrikes |url=https://www.aa.com.tr/en/middle-east/turkish-palestinian-friendship-hospital-in-gaza-severely-damaged-from-israeli-airstrikes/3037514 |work=[[Anadolu Agency]] |access-date=30 October 2023 |archive-date=30 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231030074503/https://www.aa.com.tr/en/middle-east/turkish-palestinian-friendship-hospital-in-gaza-severely-damaged-from-israeli-airstrikes/3037514 |url-status=live}}</ref> On 9 November, the Gaza government media office stated Israel had bombed eight hospitals in the past three days.<ref>{{cite news |title=Eight Gaza hospitals bombed in three days |url=https://aje.io/u6olfz?update=2473703 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=9 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240302235528/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/11/3/israel-hamas-war-live-israeli-forces-gather-outside-gaza-city?update=2460132 |archive-date=2 March 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |last1=Qarjouli |first1=Asmahan |title=Qatar's FM demands 'immediate' Gaza ceasefire as UN lashes out over civilian death toll |url=https://dohanews.co/qatars-fm-demands-immediate-gaza-ceasefire-as-un-lashes-out-over-civilian-death-toll/ |website=Doha News |date=9 November 2023 |access-date=9 November 2023 |archive-date=9 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231109152046/https://dohanews.co/qatars-fm-demands-immediate-gaza-ceasefire-as-un-lashes-out-over-civilian-death-toll/ |url-status=live}}</ref>

According to United Nations Secretary-General António Guterres, the hostilities in Gaza and Israel have “created appalling human suffering, physical destruction and collective trauma across Israel and the Occupied Palestinian Territory”.<ref name="Humanitarian impact of the conflict"/>

==== Al-Shifa Hospital ====
{{main|Al-Shifa Hospital siege}}

On 19 November, the premature babies at al-Shifa were evacuated to southern Gaza, where they were planned to be moved to Egypt the following day.<ref name="apnews.com">{{cite news |last1=Jobain |first1=Najib |last2=Magdy |first2=Samy |title=31 'very sick' babies have been evacuated from Gaza's largest hospital, where trauma patients remain |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-hamas-war-news-11-19-2023-08a2f441a9ea03bf0bb3db0de6fc5408 |work=[[Associated Press]] |date=19 November 2023 |access-date=19 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240129094303/https://apnews.com/article/israel-hamas-war-news-11-19-2023-08a2f441a9ea03bf0bb3db0de6fc5408 |archive-date=29 January 2024}}</ref> The World Health Organization stated it was planning missions to transport the remaining al-Shifa patients to [[Nasser Medical Complex]] and [[European Gaza Hospital]] in the next 2–3 days.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Diaz |first1=Jaclyn |title=31 premature babies are evacuated from Al-Shifa Hospital to southern Gaza |url=https://www.npr.org/2023/11/19/1214024420/gaza-israel-al-shifa-hospital-evacuation |work=[[NPR]] |access-date=19 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231130095757/https://www.npr.org/2023/11/19/1214024420/gaza-israel-al-shifa-hospital-evacuation |archive-date=30 November 2023}}</ref>

==== Kamal Adwan Hospital ====
{{main|Kamal Adwan Hospital siege}}
On 3 December, the IDF bombed the Kamal Adwan hospital, killing at least four people.<ref>{{cite news |first1=Edna |last1=Mohamed |first2=Farah |last2=Najjar |first3=Urooba |last3=Jamal |date=4 ==== Al-Aqsa Hospital ====
[[File:Relatives of Palestinians who died in Israeli airstrikes gathering around the bodies taken from the morgue of Al-Aqsa Martyrs hospital in Deir el-Balah, Gaza.jpg|left|thumb|Relatives of Palestinians who died in Israeli airstrikes gathering around the bodies taken from the morgue of [[Al-Aqsa Hospital massacre|Al-Aqsa hospital]] in Deir el-Balah]]
Beginning on 6 January, doctors at [[Shuhada al-Aqsa Hospital]] reported that Israeli fire was nearing the hospital. Tens of thousands of people were reported to be sheltering at the hospital.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Abu Riash |first1=Abdelhakim |title=Photos: Terrified people flee Israeli attacks at Al-Aqsa Martyrs Hospital |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/gallery/2024/1/10/photos-al-aqsa-martyrs-hospital |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=13 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240229204936/https://www.aljazeera.com/gallery/2024/1/10/photos-al-aqsa-martyrs-hospital |archive-date=29 February 2024}}</ref> British doctor [[Nick Maynard]] stated his medical team was forced to evacuate the hospital as Israeli troops attacked the hospital.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Goillandeau |first1=Martin |title=British surgeon says Gaza 'beyond worst thing' he's seen, as Jordan's king warns Israel creating a 'generation of orphans' |url=https://www.cnn.com/2024/01/09/middleeast/gaza-orphan-british-doctor-jordan-king-intl-hnk/index.html |work=[[CNN]] |date=9 January 2024 |access-date=13 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240229124201/https://www.cnn.com/2024/01/09/middleeast/gaza-orphan-british-doctor-jordan-king-intl-hnk/index.html |archive-date=29 February 2024}}</ref> [[Medical Aid for Palestinians]] and the [[International Rescue Committee]] both also evacuated their medical teams when the IDF dropped leaflets telling nearby residents they were in a "dangerous combat zone."<ref>{{cite news |title=2 medical groups say they are pulling teams from central Gaza hospital due to IDF operations |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/2-medical-groups-say-they-are-pulling-teams-from-central-gaza-hospital-due-to-idf-operations/ |work=[[Times of Israel]] |access-date=13 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240125012321/https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/2-medical-groups-say-they-are-pulling-teams-from-central-gaza-hospital-due-to-idf-operations/ |archive-date=25 January 2024}}</ref><ref name="'Deep concern' for patients and staff">{{cite news |last1=Davies |first1=Alys |title='Deep concern' for patients and staff at Gaza's al-Aqsa hospital |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67929397 |work=[[BBC News]] |date=10 January 2024 |access-date=13 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240205211823/https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67929397 |archive-date=5 February 2024}}</ref> Following a visit to the hospital, the [[World Health Organization]] found 70% of staff and many patients had fled.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Farge |first1=Emma |title=Medics, patients flee Gaza's remaining hospitals as fighting intensifies - WHO |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/medics-patients-flee-gazas-remaining-hospitals-fighting-intensifies-who-2024-01-09/ |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=13 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240414223455/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/medics-patients-flee-gazas-remaining-hospitals-fighting-intensifies-who-2024-01-09/ |archive-date=14 April 2024}}</ref> Doctors reported many patients who were physically unable to move, and that conditions were rapidly deteriorating, with one doctor stating, "A child came in alive, literally burnt to the bone, their hands were contracting. Their face was just charcoal, and they were alive and talking. And we had no morphine."<ref name="'Deep concern' for patients and staff"/><ref>{{cite news |title=Desperately trying to save children at one of Gaza's last functioning hospitals |url=https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/middle-east/israel-gaza-hospital-palestinians-hamas-b2477037.html |work=[[The Independent]] |date=11 January 2024 |access-date=13 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240212120600/https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/middle-east/israel-gaza-hospital-palestinians-hamas-b2477037.html |archive-date=12 February 2024}}</ref>

In an interview with ''[[NPR]]'' on 10 January, one American doctor described the situation at Al-Aqsa as the "stuff of nightmares".<ref>{{cite news |date=10 January 2024 |title='It's the Stuff of Nightmares' Scenes from Inside a Gaza Hospital |url=https://www.npr.org/2024/01/10/1198909954/consider-this-from-npr-draft-01-10-2024 |work=[[NPR]] |access-date=13 January 2024 |archive-date=12 Ghebreyesus]], the World Health Organization chief, stated, "Three months into this conflict, it is inconceivable that this most essential need — the protection of health care — is not assured."<ref>{{cite news |last1=Martuscelli |first1=Carlo |title=Only 5 doctors remain in one of Gaza's last hospitals, warns WHO |url=https://www.politico.eu/article/only-5-doctors-remain-one-gazas-last-hospitals-warns-who-al-aqsa/ |work=[[Politico]] |date=8 January 2024 |access-date=13 January 2024 |archive-date=13 January professionals and doctors warned of the danger of Al-Aqsa's closure since it was the last remaining hospital in the entirety of central Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Parker |first1=Claire |date=8 January 2024 |title=Displaced residents flee last hospital in central Gaza as fighting nears |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2024/01/08/israel-hamas-gaza-hospital-blinken/ |newspaper=[[The of fuel to power its generators, leading to a blackout that threatened patients.<ref>{{cite news |title=Blackout in Gaza's Al-Aqsa Hospital as fuel runs out, babies at high risk |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/1/13/blackout-in-gazas-al-aqsa-hospital-as-fuel-runs-out-babies-at-high-risk |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=13 January 2024 power cut at packed Al-Aqsa Hospital |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/5/24/israels-war-on-gaza-live-news-at-least-60-palestinians-killed-in-attacks?update=2921827 |work=[[Al Jazeera |url-status=live}}</ref>

=== Evacuation challenges ===
[[File:Fars Photo of Casualties in Gaza Strip during 2023 War 26.jpg|thumb|Medic carrying wounded Palestinian child in Gaza|alt=A man carrying a bloodied and bandaged child.]]

On 14 October, Israel ordered the evacuation of 22 hospitals in northern Gaza. The WHO described the order as a "death sentence" for the sick and wounded.<ref>{{cite news |last=Abdulrahim |first=Raja |date=15 October 2023
