=== Additional challenges ===
[[File:Gaza death graph.png|thumb|Gaza death graph]]
On 28 October, a [[communications blackout]] meant wounded civilians could not dial emergency services.<ref>{{cite web |date=28 October 2023 |title=Ambulances Unable to Reach the Wounded in Gaza Due to Communication Blackout: WHO |url=https://thewire.in/health/ambulances-unable-to-reach-the-wounded-in-palestine-due-to-communication-blackout-who |work=[[The Wire (India)|The Wire]] |access-date=29 October 2023 |archive-date=29 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231029020618/https://thewire.in/health/ambulances-unable-to-reach-the-wounded-in-palestine-due-to-communication-blackout-who |url-status=live}}</ref> Ambulances were then evenly geographically distributed to provide "faster access to the injured."<ref>{{cite news |date=28 October 2023 |title=Ambulances distributed throughout Gaza due to comms blackout |url=https://aje.io/nw7juv?update=2445098 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=29 October 2023 |archive-date=29 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231029024819/https://aje.io/nw7juv?update=2445098 |url-status=live}}</ref> A surgeon at [[Al-Ahli Arab Hospital|Al-Ahli hospital]] stated on 18 November they had run out of blood for transfusions.<ref>{{cite news |first1=Mersiha |last1=Gadzo |first2=Virginia |last2=Pietromarchi |first3=Priyanka |last3=Shankar |first4=Lyndal |last4=Rowlands |first5=John |last5=Power |date=12 November 2023 |title=Al-Ahli hospital has run out of blood: Surgeon |url=https://aje.io/bt6i03?update=2480872 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=12 November 2023 |archive-date=18 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231118163019/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/11/12/israel-gaza-war-live-israeli-army-surrounding-al-quds-hospital?update=2480872 |url-status=live}}</ref>

Doctors in south Gaza reported a lack of beds and supplies.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Khoury |first1=Jack |title=Without Equipment, Staff, or Electricity: Hospitals in Southern Gaza Strip Overwhelmed by Scale of Wounded and Ill |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-12-06/ty-article/.premium/hospitals-in-southern-gaza-strip-overwhelmed-by-scale-of-wounded-and-ill/0000018c-3e33-d11b-a3bf-febb23d70000 |work=[[Haaretz]] |access-date=9 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240313170626/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-12-06/ty-article/.premium/hospitals-in-southern-gaza-strip-overwhelmed-by-scale-of-wounded-and-ill/0000018c-3e33-d11b-a3bf-febb23d70000 |archive-date=13 March 2024}}</ref> By 8 December, an estimated 286 health workers in Gaza had been killed by Israel.<ref>{{cite web |last1=Guterres |first1=Antonio |title=Secretary-General's remarks to the Security Council - on the situation in the Middle East, including the Palestinian Question |url=https://www.un.org/sg/en/content/sg/statement/2023-12-08/secretary-generals-remarks-the-security-council-the-situation-the-middle-east-including-the-palestinian-question-bilingual-delivered-scroll-down-for-all-english |website=[[United Nations]] |access-date=10 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240314081313/https://www.un.org/sg/en/content/sg/statement/2023-12-08/secretary-generals-remarks-the-security-council-the-situation-the-middle-east-including-the-palestinian-question-bilingual-delivered-scroll-down-for-all-english |archive-date=14 March 2024}}</ref> On 4 December, Doctors Without Borders stated hospitals in southern Gaza were overflowing with wounded patients.<ref>{{cite web |title=Gaza: Hospitals in the south overflowing with hundreds of injured |url=https://msf.org.uk/article/gaza-hospitals-south-overflowing-hundreds-injured#:~:text=“With%20the%20situation%20as%20it,Forcible%20displacement%20must%20stop%20now. |website=[[Doctors Without Borders]] |access-date=5 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231221215825/https://msf.org.uk/article/gaza-hospitals-south-overflowing-hundreds-injured |archive-date=21 December 2023}}</ref> The Ministry of Health stated 50,000 people had been wounded since the start of the conflict.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Berger |first1=Miriam |title=Gaza's health system is 'on its knees' as Israel pushes into Khan Younis |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/12/10/gaza-health-israel-khan-younis/ |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]] |access-date=12 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240303230108/https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/12/10/gaza-health-israel-khan-younis/ |archive-date=3 March 2024}}</ref>

The Red Crescent stated al-Quds was completely out of service on 12 November, as Al-Shifa also stopped receiving patients.<ref>{{cite news |date=12 November 2023 |title=Al-Quds Hospital out of service: PRCS |url=https://aje.io/bt6i03?update=2480814 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=12 November 2023 |archive-date=18 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231118163020/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/11/12/israel-gaza-war-live-israeli-army-surrounding-al-quds-hospital?update=2480814 |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Burke |first1=Jason |title=Two major Gaza hospitals close to new patients as heavy fighting rages |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/nov/12/two-major-gaza-hospitals-close-new-patients-heavy-fighting-rages |work=[[The Guardian]] |date=13 November 2023 |access-date=13 November 2023 |archive-date=13 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231113011948/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/nov/12/two-major-gaza-hospitals-close-new-patients-heavy-fighting-rages |url-status=live}}</ref> On 16 November, the [[Indonesia Hospital]] completely shut down, leaving 45 patients in need of surgery.<ref>{{cite news |last=Choukeir |first=Jana |title=Gaza hospital shut down, 45 patients left needing surgery - director |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/gaza-hospital-shut-down-45-patients-left-needing-surgery-director-2023-11-16/ |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=17 November 2023 |archive-date=17 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231117003418/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/gaza-hospital-shut-down-45-patients-left-needing-surgery-director-2023-11-16/ |url-status=live}}</ref> [[UNOCHA]] stated only four small hospitals in northern Gaza and eight health facilities in southern Gaza were still functioning.<ref>{{cite web |title=Hostilities in the Gaza Strip and Israel |url=https://www.unocha.org/publications/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-50 |website=[[UNOCHA]] |date=25 November 2023 |access-date=27 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240303230047/https://www.unocha.org/publications/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-50 |archive-date=3 March 2024}}</ref> On 30 November, WHO chief [[Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus]] stated the health needs of Gaza had increased dramatically, though only one-third of its health facilities were functioning.<ref>{{cite news |date= |title=WHO chief: Health needs have increased 'dramatically' in Gaza |url=https://aje.io/ba1mme?update=2525113 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=1 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231220052157/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/11/30/israel-hamas-war-live-sixth-captive-prisoner-swap-ahead-of-truce-deadline?update=2525113 |archive-date=20 December 2023}}</ref>

On 9 January, Rik Peeperkorn, the WHO representative for Israel and Palestine, stated, "I’ve never seen so many amputees in my life, including among children. This will have such a long-term impact on everything."<ref>{{cite news |last1=Schlein |first1=Lisa |date=9 January 2024 |title=Health Catastrophe Unfolding in Gaza as Humanitarian Space Shrinks |url=https://www.voanews.com/a/health-catastrophe-unfolding-in-gaza-as-humanitarian-space-shrinks-/7432854.html |work=[[VOA]] |access-date=10 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240131030425/https://www.voanews.com/a/health-catastrophe-unfolding-in-gaza-as-humanitarian-space-shrinks-/7432854.html |archive-date=31 January 2024}}</ref> On 18 January, the United Nations reported patients were dying even while hospitalized because Gaza's remaining hospitals were overwhelmed with tens of thousands of wounded people.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Lederer |first1=Edith |title=UN: Palestinians are dying in hospitals as estimated 60,000 wounded overwhelm remaining doctors |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-un-gaza-hospitals-overwhelmed-7c6c549b4bb52f0917957bb7c4143b2d |work=[[Associated Press]] |access-date=22 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240301000841/https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-un-gaza-hospitals-overwhelmed-7c6c549b4bb52f0917957bb7c4143b2d |archive-date=1 March 2024}}</ref>

===November===
[[File:Damage in Gaza Strip during the October 2023 - 23.jpg|thumb|right|Victim of Israeli airstrike in [[Jabalia refugee camp|Jabalia]].]]

|first2=Saeed |title=The Ruined Landscape of Gaza After Nearly Three Months of Bombing |url=https://www.wsj.com/world/middle-east/gaza-destruction-bombing-israel-aa528542# |newspaper=[[The Wall Street Journal]] |access-date=30 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240627195038/https://www.wsj.com/world/middle-east/gaza-destruction-bombing-israel-aa528542 |archive-date=27 June 2024}}</ref> Torrential rains caused flooding, which raised fears of disease spread.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Snell |first1=Joe |last2=Balousha |first2=Hazem |title=Torrential rains in Gaza bring flooding and disease to displaced population |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/12/13/gaza-rain-displaced-humanitarian/ |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]] |access-date=5 January 2024 ===January===
On 5 January 2024, evacuees fleeing Israeli attacks in central Gaza stated the situation there was "hell on Earth."<ref>{{cite news |title=Continuing attacks in central Gaza creating hell on Earth |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/5/israel-war-on-gaza-live-israel-attacks-bombard-khan-younis-rafah?update=2599256 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=5 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240106012924/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/5/israel-war-on-gaza-live-israel-attacks-bombard-khan-younis-rafah?update=2599256 |archive-date=6 January 2024}}</ref> One survivor of an Israeli airstrike wrote, "Even though that air strike did not kill us, it destroyed something inside us."<ref>{{cite news |last1=Mhawish |first1=Mohammed R. |title='He's breathing': My two hours under Gaza's rubble after an Israeli strike |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/features/2024/1/5/hes-breathing-my-two-hours-under-gazas-rubble-after-an-israeli-strike |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=7 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240229152425/https://www.aljazeera.com/features/2024/1/5/hes-breathing-my-two-hours-under-gazas-rubble-after-an-israeli-strike |archive-date=29 February 2024}}</ref> On 12 January, the UN Secretary-General for Human Rights stated that at least 319 internally displaced persons were killed and 1,135 injured by Israeli airstrikes while sheltering in UN shelters.<ref>{{cite web |title=ASG Brands Kehris briefs Security Council on situation in Israel and the Occupied Palestinian Territory |url=https://www.ohchr.org/en/statements-and-speeches/2024/01/asg-brands-kehris-briefs-security-council-on-situation-israel-occupied-palestinian-territory |website=[[United Nations]] |publisher=[[OHCHR]] |access-date=13 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240228160220/https://www.ohchr.org/en/statements-and-speeches/2024/01/asg-brands-kehris-briefs-security-council-on-situation-israel-occupied-palestinian-territory |archive-date=28 February 2024}}</ref>

As of January 2024, Israel’s offensive has either damaged or destroyed 70–80% of all buildings in northern Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |title=Over 50% of Gaza buildings damaged or destroyed in Israel's bombardment |url=https://www.axios.com/2024/01/14/gaza-building-damage-israel-war |work=[[Axios (website)|Axios]] |date=5 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240226222228/https://www.axios.com/2024/01/14/gaza-building-damage-israel-war |archive-date=26 February 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=The numbers that reveal the extent of the destruction in Gaza |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/jan/08/the-numbers-that-reveal-the-extent-of-the-destruction-in-gaza |work=[[The Guardian]] |date=8 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240312155404/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/jan/08/the-numbers-that-reveal-the-extent-of-the-destruction-in-gaza |archive-date=12 March 2024}}</ref> Numerous casualties were reported in an airstrike on a residential building near [[Nasser Medical Complex]] in [[Khan Younis]], with hospital staff reporting having to bury 40 bodies on the hospital grounds.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Gritten |first1=David |title=Dozens reported killed as battle rages in Gaza's Khan Younis |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-68055933 |work=[[BBC News]] |access-date=22 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240214003728/https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-68055933 |archive-date=14 February 2024}}</ref> By 30 January, at least half of all buildings in the entirety of Gaza had been destroyed or damaged.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Palumbo |first1=Daniele |title=At least half of Gaza's buildings damaged or destroyed, new analysis shows |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-68006607 |work=[[BBC News]] |access-date=31 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240130175133/https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-68006607 |archive-date=30 January 2024}}</ref>

=== February ===

shelling, and demolitions.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Tétrault-Farber |first1=Gabrielle |title=Satellite images show 30% of Gaza destroyed, UN centre says The ''New York Times'' estimated that at least half of Gaza's buildings had been damaged or destroyed.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Abraham |first1=Leanne |last2=Erden |first2=Bora |last3=Ibrahim had destroyed 1,000 homes and rendered 560 housing units uninhabitable.<ref name="ap8" /> By 15 October, an estimated 1 million people in Gaza had been displaced, many of them fleeing northern Gaza |archive-date=29 February 2024}}</ref>}}

2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240302192958/https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/11/30/israel-hamas-war-news-gaza-hostages-update-palestine/#link-6YZ2QKUC4NDOLHZUIOEPOGV2ZY |archive-date=2 March 2024}}</ref> It issued a map of numbered zones, dividing the Gaza Strip into hundreds of different districts.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Sulliman |first1=Adela |title=IDF issues civilian 'evacuation zone map' for first time, it says |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/11/30/israel-hamas-war-news-gaza-hostages-update-palestine/#link-AZR2NLHJ3VHJTN3XFBP335G7NY 2023}}</ref> At the same time it issued the evacuation, Israel bombed Rafah.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Han |first1=Jintak |title=Photos: Explosions rock Rafah as pause for humanitarian aid expires 2023}}</ref> On 4 December, a UN representative stated "another wave of displacement is underway."<ref>{{cite web |last1=Jobain |first1=Najib |title=Israel orders evacuations as it widens offensive, military.<ref>{{cite web |title=UNRWA Situation Report #47 on the situation in the Gaza Strip and the West Bank, including East Jerusalem Rafah.<ref>{{cite web |last1=Tétrault-Farber |first1=Gabrielle |title=Gaza faces public health disaster, UN humanitarian office says |website=Reuters |access-date=14 December 2023}}</ref> On 21 December, a ''[[Financial Times]]'' analysis found Israel had left northern Gaza virtually uninhabitable.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Srivastava |archive-date=19 February 2024}}</ref>

== Communications ==
{{See also|Communications in the State of Palestine}}

Since the start of the war on 7 October, Gaza has undergone numerous [[communications blackout]]s.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Rasgon |first1=Adam |title=These Workers Are Risking Their Lives to Restore Gaza's Phone Network |work=The New York Times |date=13 March 2024 |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2024/03/13/world/middleeast/gaza-phone-networks.html?smid=nytcore-ios-share&referringSource=articleShare&sgrp=c-cb |access-date=18 March 2024}}</ref> Direct attacks on telecommunications infrastructure by Israel, electricity blockades and fuel shortages have caused the near-total collapse of Gaza's largest cell network providers.<ref name=":02">{{Cite news |last=Español |first=Marc |date=29 January 2024 |title=The Egyptians who have sent more than 130,000 digital cell phone cards to Gaza to defy blackouts |url=https://english.elpais.com/international/2024-01-29/the-egyptians-who-have-sent-more-than-130000-digital-cell-phone-cards-to-gaza-to-defy-blackouts.html |access-date=20 March 2024 |work=[[El País]] |language=en-us |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240416144411/https://english.elpais.com/international/2024-01-29/the-egyptians-who-have-sent-more-than-130000-digital-cell-phone-cards-to-gaza-to-defy-blackouts.html |archive-date=16 April 2024}}</ref><ref name="theguardian">{{Cite news |last=Aly |first=Rasha |date=17 December 2023 |title=Palestinians in Gaza using eSim cards to get around communications blackout |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/dec/17/esim-cards-internet-gaza-palestinians |access-date=19 March 2024 |work=[[The Guardian]] |language=en-GB |issn=0261-3077 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240715154212/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/dec/17/esim-cards-internet-gaza-palestinians |archive-date=15 July 2024}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last=Vo |first=Lam Thuy |date=7 November 2023 |title='Let Me Tell Them Goodbye Before They Get Killed': How eSIM Cards Are Connecting Palestinian Families – The Markup |url=https://themarkup.org/news/2023/11/07/let-me-tell-them-goodbye-before-they-get-killed-how-esims-cards-are-connecting-palestinian-families |access-date=19 March 2024 |website=themarkup.org |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240516173503/https://themarkup.org/news/2023/11/07/let-me-tell-them-goodbye-before-they-get-killed-how-esims-cards-are-connecting-palestinian-families |archive-date=16 May 2024}}</ref> Lack of internet access has obstructed Gazan citizens from communicating with loved ones, learning of IDF operations, and identifying both the areas most exposed to bombing and possible escape routes.<ref name=":02" /> The blackouts have also impeded emergency services, making it more difficult to locate and access the time-critical injured,<ref name=":02" /> and have impeded humanitarian aid agencies and journalists as well.<ref name=":02" />

On 27 October, Gaza underwent a near total communications blackout after [[Paltel Group|Paltel]]'s [[Radio masts and towers|communication towers]] were destroyed in an Israeli attack.<ref name="The Destruction of Gaza’s Internet">{{cite magazine |last1=Burgess |first1=Matt |title=The Destruction of Gaza's Internet Is Complete |url=https://www.wired.com/story/gaza-internet-blackout-israel/ |magazine=[[Wired (magazine)|Wired]] |access-date=28 October 2023 |archive-date=27 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231027234505/https://www.wired.com/story/gaza-internet-blackout-israel/ |url-status=live}}</ref> This cut off Gaza from any phone or internet service.<ref>{{cite news |title=Near-total internet and cellular blackout hits Gaza as Israel ramps up strikes |url=https://www.nbcnews.com/tech/internet/internet-blackout-hits-gaza-israel-ramps-strikes-rcna122531 |work=[[NBC News]] |date=27 October 2023 |access-date=28 October 2023 |archive-date=27 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231027175159/https://www.nbcnews.com/tech/internet/internet-blackout-hits-gaza-israel-ramps-strikes-rcna122531 |url-status=live}}</ref> As a result, humanitarian groups, including UNICEF, WHO, the [[Palestine Red Crescent Society]], Doctors Without Borders, [[American Friends Service Committee]], Medical Aid for Palestinians, and [[ActionAid]] lost all contact with their staff.<ref name="What aid groups have lost">{{cite news |title=What aid groups have lost contact with Gaza staff? |url=https://aje.io/i5z284?update=2442524 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=28 October 2023 |archive-date=18 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231118165231/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/10/27/israel-hamas-war-live-israel-bombs-gaza-overnight-more-than-7000-dead?update=2442524 |url-status=live}}</ref> The Palestinian Red Crescent Society stated wounded people would no longer be able to dial Gaza's [[Emergency telephone number|emergency number]] for an ambulance.<ref name="Phone Network Cut">{{cite web |title=Internet, Phone Network Cut Across Gaza |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/hamas-govt-says-internet-communications-cut-across-gaza-9b062c6f it was "deeply concerned" about the ability of [[medic]]s to provide care, stating it had lost all contact with operations room and staff in Gaza.<ref name="Phone Network Cut" /> On 28 October, [[Elon Musk]] offered to provide humanitarian groups with [[Starlink]] access, but [[Shlomo Karhi]] stated Israel would fight it with every "means at its disposal” because Hamas will use it for terrorist activities.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Ruhiyyih Ewing |first1=Giselle |title=Musk says Starlink will support connectivity to aid organizations in Gaza |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Israeli official says will fight Starlink's deployment in Gaza |url=https://aje.io/nw7juv?update=2444873 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] The UN Assistant Secretary-General and Humanitarian Coordinator in the Occupied Palestinian Territory, Lynn Hastings,<ref>{{cite web |last1=Lynn |first1=Hastings |title=Lynn Hastings, Assistant |url-status=live}}</ref> The [[Committee to Protect Journalists]] warned the world was "losing a window into the reality" of the situation in Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Shurafa |first1=Wafaa |last2=Federman |first2=Josef |last3=Mroue |first3=Bassem |title=Israel steps up air and ground attacks in Gaza and cuts off the territory's communications |url-status=live}}</ref> [[Michael Lynk]], a former [[United Nations special rapporteur|UN rapporteur]], stated one purpose of the internet blackout was to keep "the world blinded on what's Marwa Fatafta, policy manager of [[Access Now]], stated that "taking Gaza completely off the grid while launching an unprecedented bombardment campaign only means something atrocious is about to happen."<ref name="The Destruction of Gaza’s Internet" /> On 28 October, [[Netblocks]] stated Gaza's telephone and internet communications were gradually returning.<ref>{{cite news |title=Netblocks |url-status=live}}</ref> On 31 October, Fatafta stated the blackout had been used by Israel to cover up potential [[War crimes in the Gaza war|war crimes]] as they began their [[Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip (2023–present)|ground invasion]] and called it a "warfare tactic to induce more pain on the population."<ref name="warfare tactic" /> Paltel announced Gaza had again been cut off from telecommunications and internet service.<ref name="warfare tactic">{{cite news |title=Internet shutdowns a 'warfare tactic': Rights group |url=https://aje.io/cevgx6?update=2453099 |work=[[Al Jazeera |url-status=live}}</ref> On 3 November, the [[BBC]] began broadcasting an [[Gaza Daily|emergency radio service]] on [[Medium wave|mediumwave]] from [[Cyprus]] in attempt to retain communications with Gazan civilians and support information-finding such as "where to access shelter, food and water supplies".<ref>{{Cite news |title=BBC World Service announces Emergency Radio Service for Gaza |url=https://aje.io/yu4f6n?update=2492242 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=16 November 2023 |archive-date=18 November 2023 |url-status=live}}</ref> The following day, communications were restored after a limited quantity of fuel was allowed to enter the Gaza Strip.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Parker |first1=Claire == Humanitarian aid ==

===Initial block on aid===
{{Rquote|right|The amount of aid coming in is a drop in the bucket of Gaza’s humanitarian needs. Before this conflict, about 100 trucks of aid alone entered Gaza [a day]. So imagine now, with all the hostilities going on, if only this number is coming in.|Mey al Sayegh, ([[International Federation of Red Cross and Red Crescent Societies|Red Cross]])<ref>{{cite news |last1=Español |first1=Marc |title=Only a trickle of humanitarian aid entering Gaza: 'It's a drop in the bucket' |url=https://english.elpais.com/international/2023-11-10/only-a-trickle-of-humanitarian-aid-entering-gaza-its-a-drop-in-the-bucket.html |work=[[El País]] |date=10 November 2023 |access-date=10 November 2023 |archive-date=10 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231110185025/https://english.elpais.com/international/2023-11-10/only-a-trickle-of-humanitarian-aid-entering-gaza-its-a-drop-in-the-bucket.html |url-status=live}}</ref>}}

On 9 October, Israel implemented a [[October 2023 Israeli blockade of the Gaza Strip|complete blockade]] on Gaza, preventing the entry of any humanitarian aid.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Federman |first1=Josef |last2=Adwan |first2=Issam |title=Israeli defense minister orders 'complete siege' on Gaza after Hamas surprise attack |url=https://www.pbs.org/newshour/world/israeli-defense-minister-orders-complete-siege-on-gaza-after-hamas-surprise-attack |work=[[PBS Newshour]] |date=9 October 2023 |access-date=19 October 2023 Egypt closed its border to prevent civilians fleeing, but said that it would allow aid to be delivered through the [[Rafah crossing]].<ref>{{cite news |title=Egypt says Israel seeks to empty Gaza, rejects corridors for civilians |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/12/egypt-says-israel-seeks-to-empty-gaza-rejects-corridors-for-civilians |access-date=13 October 2023 |work=[[Al Jazeera later, despite international calls for deliveries, hundreds of tons of aid were stuck on Egypt's side of the border, as Israel bombarded the crossing amid fears of weapons deliveries, and declined to assure Egyptian authorities it would pause airstrikes for civilian aid convoys.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Mohamed |first1=Yusri |last2=Awadalla |first2=Nadine |last3=Ramadan |first3=Tala |date=16 October In Israel, aid to Gaza was reportedly prevented by far-right politicians allied with Netanyahu.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Yasmeen |first1=Abutaleb |last2=Pager |first2=Tyler |last3=Hudson |first3=John ===Issues with delivery===
{{See also|Structural violence}}[[File:Humanitarian crisis in Gaza Strip following 2023 total blockade by Israel 2.png|thumb|Trucks with [[humanitarian aid]] waiting to cross from Egypt into the Gaza Strip]]
On 27 October, Lynn Hastings, the UN's humanitarian coordinator for Palestine, stated Israel opposed the delivery of humanitarian aid to northern Gaza.<ref name="Israel 'clearly' opposes aid">{{cite news |first1=Joseph |last1=Stepansky |first2=Farah |last2=Najjar |date=27 October 2023 |title=Israel 'clearly' opposes aid deliveries: UN |url=https://aje.io/i5z284?update=2440761 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=27 October 2023 |archive-date=18 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231118165748/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/10/27/israel-hamas-war-live-israel-bombs-gaza-overnight-more-than-7000-dead?update=2440761 |url-status=live}}</ref> As a result, UN staff would need to risk their own lives if it was determined such aid would be "lifesaving" to people in need.<ref name="Israel 'clearly' opposes aid" /> [[Philippe Lazzarini]] stated "soon many more will die" from Israel's blockade.<ref>{{cite news |first1=Joseph |last1=Stepansky |first2=Farah |last2=Najjar |date=27 October 2023 |title='Soon many more will die' from Gaza siege: UN |url=https://aje.io/i5z284?update=2440700 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=27 October 2023 |archive-date=18 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231118165745/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/10/27/israel-hamas-war-live-israel-bombs-gaza-overnight-more-than-7000-dead?update=2440700 |url-status=live}}</ref>

When asked about Hamas's responsibility for the safety of civilians, Hamas leader [[Mousa Abu Marzook]] allegedly replied that "it is the responsibility of the [[United Nations]] to protect them... [and] it is the responsibility of the occupation to provide them with... services".<ref>{{Cite news |last=Halabi |first=Einav |date=31 October 2023 |title=Senior Hamas official: 'Tunnels are for us, the UN can take care of Palestinian citizens' |language=en |work=[[Ynetnews]] |url=https://www.ynetnews.com/article/bk00giq0fa |access-date=7 November 2023 |archive-date=4 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231104222608/https://www.ynetnews.com/article/bk00giq0fa |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=Pacchiani |first=Gianluca |title=Top Hamas official declares group is not responsible for defending Gazan civilians |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/top-hamas-official-claims-group-is-not-responsible-for-defending-gazan-civilians/ |access-date=7 November 2023 |work=[[Times of Israel]] |language=en-US |archive-date=6 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231106025008/https://www.timesofisrael.com/top-hamas-official-claims-group-is-not-responsible-for-defending-gazan-civilians/ |url-status=live}}</ref> On 28 October, ''The New York Times'' reported that Hamas had stockpiled food, water, medicine and sanitary products in underground caches, in amounts that would allow it to continue fighting for several months without resupply.<ref name=":0">{{Cite news |last1=Rosenberg |first1=Matthew |last2=Abi-Habib |first2=Maria |date=27 October 2023 |title=As Gazans Scrounge for Food and Water, Hamas Sits on a 12 November, ''[[Kan 11]]'' aired a video taken by a Gazan civilian, that appeared to show Hamas policemen beating civilians approaching a truck carrying humanitarian aid for food, before allegedly taking the supplies for themselves.<ref>{{Cite news |date=12 November 2023 |title=Footage from Gaza shows Hamas members beating up residents trying to get food |work=[[Times of Israel]] |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/footage-from-gaza-shows-hamas-members-beating-up-residents-trying-to-get-food/ |access-date=18 November 2023 |archive-date=18 November 2023 Egyptian Foreign Minister [[Sameh Shoukry]] stated "Israeli obstacles" were impeding the delivery of humanitarian aid.<ref>{{cite news |first1=Umut |last1=Uras |first2=Priyanka |last2=Shankar ===Delivery during temporary ceasefire===
The amount of aid entering Gaza increased during the [[2023 Israel–Hamas ceasefire|temporary November ceasefire]].<ref>{{cite web |title=UN delivers more aid into Gaza on first day of humanitarian pause |url=https://news.un.org/en/story/2023/11/1143957 |website=UN News |date=24 November 2023 |publisher=[[United Nations]] |access-date=25 November 2023}}</ref> On 26 November, the largest shipment Philippe Lazzarini stated the aid entering Gaza was still inadequate.<ref>{{cite news |title=UNRWA chief: current state of Gaza aid 'hardly enough for humanitarian response' |title=Today, @WFP and @UNICEF had a joint mission to deliver vital food assistance to Al-Ahli hospital & surrounding areas.}}</ref> On 28 November, the [[White House]] reported that over 2,000 trucks of aid had entered Gaza since 21 October.<ref>{{Cite web |last=House |first=The White |date=28 November 2023 |title=Statement from National Security Advisor Jake Sullivan on Airlift of Critical |archive-date=28 November 2023}}</ref>

===Resumption of hostilities===
Following the resumption of hostilities on 1 December, aid deliveries into Gaza ceased.<ref>{{cite news |first1=Farah |last1=Najjar |first2=Adam |last2=Muro |date=1 December 2023 |title=No aid crossing into Gaza amid Israeli air attacks |url=https://aje.io/envkfc?update=2527079 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=1 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240312024722/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/12/1/israel-hamas-war-live-relief-and-joy-as-more-palestinian-prisoners-freed?update=2527079 |archive-date=12 March 2024}}</ref> The IDF informed the [[Palestinian Red Crescent]] that the entry of trucks was "prohibited, starting from today" until further notice.<ref>{{cite news |first1=Farah |last1=Najjar |first2=Adam |last2=Muro |date=1 December 2023 |title=Israel preventing aid trucks from entering Gaza via Rafah border crossing, PRCS says |url=https://aje.io/envkfc?update=2528166 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=1 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240312024718/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/12/1/israel-hamas-war-live-relief-and-joy-as-more-palestinian-prisoners-freed?update=2528166 |archive-date=12 March 2024}}</ref> Later the same day, the United States announced they had requested a reversal of the decision, and Israel stated it was prepared to allow aid at pre-pause levels.<ref>{{cite news |last=DeYoung |first=Karen |title=Aid shipments into Gaza to resume, U.S. says, but at pre-pause levels |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/11/30/israel-hamas-war-news-gaza-hostages-update-palestine/#link-ABE45RAE5ZHXHCQZDOHLEQFEYA |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]] |access-date=1 December 2023}}</ref> On 4 December, the United Nations Office for the Coordination of Humanitarian Affairs (OCHA) stated that approximately 100 humanitarian aid trucks and 69,000 litres of fuel entered Gaza on 3 December and 4 December. This was “well below” the on average 170 trucks and 110,000 litres of fuel that were delivered daily during the temporary ceasefire.<ref>{{Cite web |date=4 December 2023 |title=United Nations Office for the Coordination of Humanitarian Affairs - occupied Palestinian territory {{!}} Hostilities in the Gaza Strip and Israel {{!}} Flash Update #59 |url=http://www.ochaopt.org/content/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-59 |access-date=6 December 2023 |website=[[United Nations Office for the Coordination of Humanitarian Affairs]] - occupied Palestinian territory |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240719143338/https://www.ochaopt.org/content/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-59 |archive-date=19 July 2024}}</ref> On 4 December, Lynn Hastings, a UN humanitarian coordinator, stated, "The conditions required to deliver aid to the people of Gaza do not exist" and warned of a "hellish scenario" in which aid delivery was entirely impossible.<ref>{{cite news |title=WHO reports Israeli army's directive to evacuate aid warehouse in southern Gaza |archive-date=5 December 2023}}</ref>{{efn|Shortly after these comments, the Israeli government revoked Hastings' visa<ref>{{cite news |last1=Lazaroff |first1=Tozah |title=Israel revokes UN [[Martin Griffiths]] stating an immediate ceasefire was needed for the UN to continue humanitarian operations.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Ackerman |first1=Gwen |title=Israel Rebuffs Calls to Halt Gaza War as Forces Move South |url=https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2023-12-05/un-says-no-safe-place-in-gaza-as-about-1-000-killed-since-truce |work=[[Bloomberg News]] |access-date=6 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240803161629/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/12/19/israel-hamas-war-live-multinational-red-sea-force-announced-after-attacks?update=2567740 |archive-date=3 August 2024}}</ref> UN chief Antonio Guterres stated the way Israel was conducting its offensive was creating obstacles for delivery.<ref>{{cite web |title=Hostilities in the Gaza Strip and Israel Flash #76 |url=https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-76 |website=[[ReliefWeb]] |date=23 December 2023 2024}}</ref> On 29 December, Israel fired on a humanitarian aid truck marked with U.N. insignia.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Abdulrahim |first1=Raja |title=U.N. Says Israeli Forces Fired on Aid Convoy in Central Gaza |work=[[The New York Times]] |date=29 December 2023 |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/12/29/world/middleeast/un-israel-gaza-aid.html |access-date=30 December 2023}}</ref> Israel announced on 31 December it was prepared to allow aid ships from [[Cyprus]] to enter Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Williams |first1=Dan |title=Israel says it's ready to let ships bring aid to Gaza |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israel-ready-let-ships-bring-aid-gazas-shores-minister-2023-12-31/#:~:text=JERUSALEM%2C%20Dec%2031%20(Reuters),European%20countries%20as%20potential%20participants. |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=31 December 2023}}</ref> France and Jordan airdropped aid on 5 January.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Pineau |first1=Elizabeth |title=French, Jordanian airforces drop medical aid to Gaza - Elysee |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/french-jordanian-airforces-drop-medical-aid-gaza-elysee-2024-01-05/ |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=5 January 2024}}</ref> On 11 January, Samer AbdelJaber, a [[World Food Programme]] director, stated the organization had delivered "crucial food assistance to thousands of people facing catastrophic hunger" in [[Gaza City]] for the first time in weeks.<ref>{{Cite tweet |user=SamerWFP |number=1745538014426599883 |title=For the first time in weeks, @WFP was able to deliver crucial food assistance to thousands of people facing catastrophic hunger in the center of #Gaza city.}}</ref>

On 13 January 2024, UNOCHA reported the amount of aid Israel was allowing into Israel had significantly deceased since the prior month.<ref>{{cite web |title=Hostilities in the Gaza Strip and Israel Flash Update #91 |url=https://www.ochaopt.org/content/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-91 |website=[[UNOCHA]] |date=12 January 2024 |access-date=14 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240226113121/https://www.ochaopt.org/content/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-91 |archive-date=26 February 2024}}</ref> Omar Shakir, [[Human Rights Watch]]'s Israel-Palestine director, stated, "This is a deliberate Israeli government policy. Aid is not reaching north Gaza."<ref>{{cite news |title='Lives hang in the balance' amid dire humanitarian situation in Gaza: HRW |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/13/israels-war-on-gaza-live-un-fears-mass-transfer-of-palestinians-from-gaza?update=2616104 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=14 January 2024}}</ref> U.S. senators [[Chris Van Hollen]] and [[Jeff Merkley]] criticized Israel's inspection of humanitarian aid as "arbitrary" and "broken".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Keath |first1=Lee |title=Cumbersome process and 'arbitrary' Israeli inspections slow aid delivery into Gaza, US senators say |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-gaza-rafah-aid-us-senators-2bc2a3c5e5f8af8e2d3f0b7242c1a885# |work=[[Associated Press]] |date=6 January 2024 |access-date=14 January 2024}}</ref> A joint statement by the heads of [[UNICEF]], [[World Health Organization|WHO]], and the World Food Programme stated the limited quantity of aid arriving in Gaza was unable to prevent the "deadly combination of hunger, malnutrition, and disease".<ref>{{cite web |title=Preventing famine and deadly disease outbreak in Gaza requires faster, safer aid access and more supply routes |url=https://www.who.int/news/item/15-01-2024-preventing-famine-and-deadly-disease-outbreak-in-gaza-requires-faster--safer-aid-access-and-more-supply-routes#:~:text=The%20United%20Nations%2C%20international%20aid,of%20hunger%2C%20malnutrition%2C%20and%20disease |website=[[World Health Organization]] |access-date=16 January 2024}}</ref> A viral video showed huge crowds of hungry people rushing toward a rumored relief truck.<ref>{{cite news |last1=McDowall |first1=Angus |title=Video shows chaos of aid delivery on Gaza beach |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/video-shows-chaos-aid-delivery-gaza-beach-2024-01-15/ |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=16 January 2024}}</ref> On 16 January, a deal was reached between Israel and Hamas to bring more aid into Gaza.<ref>{{cite web |title=Israel and Hamas agree deal on medicine for hostages and more aid for Gaza, says Qatar |url=https://www.france24.com/en/middle-east/20240116-🔴-live-israel-says-war-to-wind-down-in-southern-gaza-as-toll-tops-24-000 |website=France24 |date=16 January 2024 |access-date=17 January 2024}}</ref> On 19 January, UNOCHA reported that nearly 70% of its aid deliveries to northern Gaza had been denied by Israel.<ref>{{cite web |title=Humanitarian Access Snapshot - North of Wadi Gaza Mid-January 2024 |url=https://www.ochaopt.org/content/humanitarian-access-snapshot-north-wadi-gaza-mid-january-2024#:~:text=The%20first%20two%20weeks%20of,scale%2Dup%20of%20humanitarian%20operations. |website=[[UNOCHA]] |date=19 January 2024 |publisher=[[United Nations]] |access-date=20 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240208130813/https://www.ochaopt.org/content/humanitarian-access-snapshot-north-wadi-gaza-mid-january-2024 |archive-date=8 February 2024}}</ref> On 29 January, the United Nations reported that Israel had denied 29 aid missions to northern Gaza.<ref>{{cite web |title=Hostilities in the Gaza Strip and Israel Flash Update #104 |url=https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-104-enarhe |website=[[ReliefWeb]] |date=29 January 2024 |publisher=[[UNOCHA]] |access-date=30 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240219170535/https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-104-enarhe |archive-date=19 February 2024}}</ref>

In late-January, at least 15 countries announced they were [[UNRWA October 7 controversy|suspending funding for UNRWA]].<ref>{{cite web |last1=Hammer |first1=Mathias |title=More than a dozen countries are suspending funds to UNRWA over alleged Hamas links |url=https://www.semafor.com/article/01/29/2024/more-than-a-dozen-countries-suspend-unrwa-funds-over-alleged-hamas-links |website=Semafor |date=29 January 2024 |access-date=30 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240209051550/https://www.semafor.com/article/01/29/2024/more-than-a-dozen-countries-suspend-unrwa-funds-over-alleged-hamas-links |archive-date=9 February 2024}}</ref> Philippe Lazarrini, the agency chief, stated, "Our humanitarian operation, on which 2 million people depend as a lifeline in Gaza, is collapsing."<ref>{{cite news |date=28 January 2024 |title=9 nations suspend contributions to UNWRA due to Oct. 7 allegations |url=https://abcnews.go.com/International/live-updates/israel-gaza-hamas-war/?id=106553905#106737867 |work=[[ABC News (United States)|ABC News]] |access-date=28 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240627145711/https://abcnews.go.com/International/live-updates/israel-gaza-hamas-war/?id=106553905#106737867 |archive-date=27 June 2024}}</ref> The regional director of [[Doctors Without Borders]] stated, "If you stop these trucks, people will die of hunger and very quickly".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Ebrahim |first1=Nadeen |title=The demise of the UN's Palestinian agency could spell disaster for millions. Here's why Israel wants it dismantled |url=https://www.cnn.com/2024/01/29/middleeast/unrwa-funding-israel-war-mime-intl/index.html# |work=[[CNN]] |date=29 January 2024 |access-date=30 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240513194203/https://www.cnn.com/2024/01/29/middleeast/unrwa-funding-israel-war-mime-intl/index.html |archive-date=13 May 2024}}</ref> UNRWA warned that without continued funding, it would be forced to cease operations by the end of February 2024.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Tétrault-Farber |first1=Gabrielle |title=What is UNRWA and why are some countries suspending its funding? |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/what-is-unrwa-un-palestinian-refugee-agency-2024-01-29/ |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=31 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240426162616/https://www.reuters.com/world/what-is-unrwa-un-palestinian-refugee-agency-2024-01-29/ |archive-date=26 April 2024}}</ref>

===Killing of aid workers===
{{See also|Societal breakdown in the Gaza Strip during the Gaza war}}

From 7 October to 17 December, 135 [[United Nations]] relief workers were killed in the Gaza Strip, making it the deadliest conflict for UN workers in world history.<ref>{{cite web |title=Complete communication blackout for four days and counting makes aid distribution in Gaza near impossible |url=https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/complete-communication-blackout-four-days-and-counting-makes-aid-distribution-gaza-near-impossible |website=[[ReliefWeb]] |date=17 December 2023 |publisher=[[Save the Children]] |access-date=18 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240312025733/https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/complete-communication-blackout-four-days-and-counting-makes-aid-distribution-gaza-near-impossible |archive-date=12 March 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Atay Alam |first1=Hande |title=UN mourns the deaths of more than 100 aid workers in Gaza, the highest number killed in any conflict in its history |url=https://www.cnn.com/2023/11/14/middleeast/united-nations-staff-deaths-gaza-intl-hnk/index.html |work=[[CNN]] |date=14 November 2023 |access-date=18 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240605222357/https://edition.cnn.com/2023/11/14/middleeast/united-nations-staff-deaths-gaza-intl-hnk/index.html |archive-date=5 June 2024}}</ref> According to Jeremy Konyndyk, the president of [[Refugees International]], "The U.S. concern about these casualties remains almost purely rhetorical. There is no policy leverage being put behind it whatsoever. Beyond expressing concern and expressing regret, that’s where it stops."<ref>{{cite news |last1=Hudson |first1=John |title=Killing of USAID contractor in Gaza fuels internal protest |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2023/12/16/usaid-contractor-hani-jnena-killed-gaza/ |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]] |access-date=18 December 2023 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240416030429/https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2023/12/16/usaid-contractor-hani-jnena-killed-gaza/ |archive-date=16 April 2024}}</ref> On 24 February 2024, the U.S. asked Israel to cease killing police in Gaza, stating it was exacerbating the crisis and leading to a "total breakdown of law and order".<ref>{{cite web |last1=Ravid |first1=Barak |title=U.S. officials warn: Gaza "is turning into Mogadishu" |url=https://www.axios.com/2024/02/24/gaza-humanitarian-aid-israel-hamas-police-biden# |website=[[Axios (website)|Axios]] |date=24 February 2024 |access-date=25 February 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240611171224/https://www.axios.com/2024/02/24/gaza-humanitarian-aid-israel-hamas-police-biden |archive-date=11 June 2024}}</ref>

== Impact on children ==
{{main|Effect of the Gaza war on children in the Gaza Strip}}

Due to over 40% of Gaza’s population being 14 or under, children have been notably impacted by Israel's attack.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Kekatos |first1=Mary |title=Why women, children are disproportionately impacted by the conflict in Gaza: Experts |url=https://abcnews.go.com/International/women-children-disproportionately-impacted-conflict-gaza-experts/story?id=104655493 |work=[[ABC News (United States)|ABC News]] |access-date=19 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240711174108/https://abcnews.go.com/International/women-children-disproportionately-impacted-conflict-gaza-experts/story?id=104655493 |archive-date=11 July 2024}}</ref> On 13 November, UNICEF stated more than 700,000 children in Gaza were [[Forced displacement|displaced]].<ref>{{cite web |title=In Gaza, more than 700,000 children have been displaced - forced to leave everything behind. |url=https://twitter.com/UNICEF/status/1724155268148191524?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw%7Ctwcamp%5Etweetembed%7Ctwterm%5E1724155268148191524%7Ctwgr%5E78a7cd78ba86ee0532e86d8148dc1907f48297a9%7Ctwcon%5Es1_&ref_url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.aljazeera.com%2Fnews%2Fliveblog%2F2023%2F11%2F13%2Fisrael-hamas-war-live-gazas-two-largest-hospitals-shut-amid-nonstop-raids |website=X post by UNICEF |publisher=[[UNICEF]] |access-date=13 November 2023}}</ref> The [[Palestine Red Crescent Society]] stated displaced children were suffering, due to power outages, lack of basic essentials, and "scenes of pain and fear."<ref>{{cite news |date= |title=PRCS tries to 'alleviate suffering of displaced children' |url=https://aje.io/bt6i03?update=2480667 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=12 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231216015928/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/11/12/israel-gaza-war-live-israeli-army-surrounding-al-quds-hospital?update=2480667 |archive-date=16 December 2023}}</ref> [[Catherine M. Russell]], the executive director of [[UNICEF]], toured Gaza on 15 November, stating many children were buried under rubble and lacking medical care.<ref>{{cite news |title=First Person: UNICEF chief in Gaza visit, bears witness to grave violations against children |url=https://news.un.org/en/story/2023/11/1143617 |website=UN News |date=15 November 2023 |publisher=[[United Nations]] |access-date=15 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231130014259/https://news.un.org/en/story/2023/11/1143617 |archive-date=30 November 2023}}</ref> Dr. Ahmed al-Fara, the head of pediatrics at [[Nasser Hospital|Nasser Medical Complex]] in [[Khan Younis]], stated due to the lack of clean water, he was witnessing the "most serious epidemic of [[gastroenteritis]]" among children he had ever seen.<ref>{{cite web |date= |title=Overcrowding at hospitals grows as more move south |url=https://aje.io/yu4f6n?update=2491642 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=16 |archive-date=3 March 2024}}</ref> UNICEF spokesperson Toby Fricker stated, "There is no safe place for children anywhere across the strip right now."<ref>{{cite news |date= |title='No place safe for children in Gaza': UNICEF |url=https://aje.io/bt6i03?update=2480844 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=12 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240316095255/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/11/12/israel-gaza-war-live-israeli-army-surrounding-al-quds-hospital?update=2480844 limbs, which would result in a lifetime of medical needs.<ref>{{cite web |date= 7 January 2024|title=Gaza: More Than 10 Children a Day Lose a Limb in Three Months of Brutal Conflict December, UNOCHA stated 50 percent of all children in the Gaza Strip were experiencing dehydration, malnutrition, respiratory and skin diseases.<ref>{{cite web |title=Hostilities in the Gaza Strip and Israel Flash Update #79 |url=https://www.ochaopt.org/content/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-79 |website=[[UNOCHA]] |date=28 December 2023 |publisher=[[United Nations]] |access-date=29 representative stated the organization was having difficulty delivering childhood vaccines.<ref>{{cite news |date=1 January 2024 |title=Vaccines received, but getting them to babies across Gaza is impossible: UN |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/1/israel-hamas-war-live-new-year-in-gaza-under-non-stop-israeli-bombardment?update=2591421 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |archive-date=5 February 2024}}</ref> On 3 January 2024, UNICEF chief Catherine M. Russell stated many children in Gaza were facing [[Global Acute Malnutrition|severe acute malnutrition]].<ref>{{cite news |date=3 January 2024 |title='Time is running out' to save children in Gaza from malnutrition, says UNICEF head |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/3/israel-hamas-war-live-hezbollah-vows-revenge-for-israeli-strike-on-beirut?update=2596539 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=3 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240226130457/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/3/israel-hamas-war-live-hezbollah-vows-revenge-for-israeli-strike-on-beirut?update=2596539 |archive-date=26 February 2024}}</ref> On 5 January, UNICEF found 90 percent of children under the age of two were eating two or fewer food groups a day.<ref>{{cite news |title=Nutrition needs of children, pregnant women in Gaza are going unmet, UNICEF says |url=https://www.pbs.org/newshour/world/nutrition-needs-of-children-pregnant-women-in-gaza-are-going-unmet-unicef-says |work=[[PBS NewsHour]] |date=5 January 2024 |agency=[[Associated Press]] |access-date=5 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240626222018/https://www.pbs.org/newshour/world/nutrition-needs-of-children-pregnant-women-in-gaza-are-going-unmet-unicef-says |archive-date=26 June 2024}}</ref>

On 6 January 2024, Tanya Haj-Hassan, a doctor with [[Doctors Without Borders]], stated children in Gaza were "dying in every way possible."<ref>{{cite web |first1=Linah |last1=Alsaafin |first2=Brian |last2=Osgood |date=6 January 2024 |title=Children in Gaza dying 'in every way possible' |archive-date=29 December 2023}}</ref> A report by Save the Children on 12 January stated children were "enduring unspeakable horrors, including life-changing injuries, burns, disease, inadequate medical care, and losing their parents and other loved ones".<ref>{{cite web |date= 11 January 2024|title=More than 10,000 children killed in Gaza in nearly 100 days of war ===Birth and pregnancy===
{{further|Women in the Gaza war#Gaza Strip}}

An estimated 150 babies were born in Gaza per day since the start of the conflict.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Collier |first1=Neil |title='A Horror Film': Mothers in Gaza on Giving Birth in a War Zone |work=[[The New York Times]] |date=20 November 2023 |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/11/20/world/middleeast/palestinian-pregnant-women-childbirth-gaza.html |access-date=27 November 2023}}</ref> A pediatric doctor at the Emirati Hospital in [[Rafah]], stated the number of premature babies born in Gaza had risen sharply.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Alsaafin |first1=Linah |last2=Humaid |first2=Maram |date=15 December 2023 |title=Emaciated but alive: Gaza mothers, premature babies reunited in Egypt [[Infant|Newborn babies]] receiving specialized care in the [[West Bank]] were separated from their mothers who were trapped in Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Loveluck |first1=Louisa |last2=Taha babies were dying from preventable diseases such as infection, [[hypothermia]], diarrhea, and [[dehydration]].<ref>{{cite web |title=The Devastating Brunt Of Conflict On Gaza's Women And Girls |url=https://www.oxfam.ca/story/the-devastating-brunt-of-conflict-on-gaza-women-and-girls |website=[[Oxfam]] |date=25 November 2023 |access-date=7 December 2023 |archive-date=18 December 2023}}</ref> Newborn babies born during the conflict died in airstrikes, though some were rescued from the rubble.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Salem |first1=Mohammed |date=12 December 2023 |title=Born and killed in Gaza war: grandmother weeps for one-month-old Idres 2023}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |first1=Linah |last1=Alsaafin |first2=Adam |last2=Muro |first3=Joseph |last3=Stepansky |date=20 December 2023 |title=3-day-old baby saved following Israeli air raid on representative had ever witnessed, as there were 180 women giving birth daily, sometimes on the streets of Gaza, as the territory's health system collapsed.<ref>{{cite news |first1=Ali |last1=Harb |first2=Brian |last2=Osgood |date=18 January 2024 |title='Worst nightmare': Giving birth in Gaza |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/18/israels-war-on-gaza-live-medicine-arrives-for-captives-palestinians?update=2630177 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=19 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240810142736/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/18/israels-war-on-gaza-live-medicine-arrives-for-captives-palestinians?update=2630177 |archive-date=10 August 2024}}</ref> On 17 January, [[Care International]] reported a 300 percent increase in the rate of [[miscarriage]] in Gaza since the start of Israel's bombing.<ref>{{cite web |access-date=20 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240622085204/https://www.unicef.org/press-releases/born-hell |archive-date=22 June 2024}}</ref> UNICEF described each birth as a #98 |url=https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/hostilities-gaza-strip-and-israel-flash-update-98-enarhe |website=[[ReliefWeb]] |date=22 January 2024 |publisher=[[UNOCHA]] Gaza conflict: UN Women |url=https://news.un.org/en/story/2024/01/1145707 |website=UN News |date=19 January 2024 |publisher=[[United Nations]] |access-date=21 January 2024 stillbirths.<ref>{{cite web |date=3 November 2023 |title=Women and newborns bearing the brunt of the conflict in Gaza, UN agencies warn |url=https://www.who.int/news/item/03-11-2023-women-and-newborns-bearing-the-brunt-of-the-conflict-in-gaza-un-agencies-warn |website=[[World Health Organization]] |access-date=24 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240801024723/https://www.who.int/news/item/03-11-2023-women-and-newborns-bearing-the-brunt-of-the-conflict-in-gaza-un-agencies-warn |archive-date=1 August 2024}}</ref>

[[Doctors Without Borders]] stated that women were giving birth in plastic tents, and that those undergoing [[C-sections]] were being released within hours.<ref name="Displaced pregnant women">{{cite web |date=29 January 2024 |title=Displaced pregnant women at high risk amid dire conditions in Rafah |url=https://www.msf.org/gaza-displaced-pregnant-women-high-risk-amid-dire-conditions-rafah |website=[[Doctors Without Borders]] |access-date=30 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240510024607/https://www.msf.org/gaza-displaced-pregnant-women-high-risk-amid-dire-conditions-rafah |archive-date=10 May 2024}}</ref> It also reported that women were being turned away from hospitals due to overcrowding, with some forced to birth in public restrooms.<ref name="Displaced pregnant women"/>

===Premature babies===
{{main|2023 Gaza Strip preterm births}}
[[File:Premature_babies_in_Gaza,_2023.webp|thumb|Premature babies at Al-Shifa.]]

The plight of Gaza's premature babies gained global attention.<ref>{{cite news |date= |title=Premature babies evacuated from Al-Shifa Hospital, health officials say |url=https://www.cbc.ca/news/world/israel-hamas-war-gaza-day-44-1.7033192 |work=[[Canadian Broadcasting Corporation|CBC]] |access-date=19 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240204074047/https://www.cbc.ca/news/world/israel-hamas-war-gaza-day-44-1.7033192 |archive-date=4 February 2024}}</ref> In late October, Gaza's premature babies faced a critical situation as [[Medical Aid for Palestinians]] and [[UNICEF]] warned that 130 infants were at risk of death due to a hospital fuel shortage caused by Israel's siege.<ref name="Medical Aid for Palestinians"/><ref name="aljazeera.com"/> The lack of fuel led to power outages, endangering premature babies in neonatal intensive care units (NICUs).<ref name="abcnews.go.com"/><ref name="ABC News"/> Despite assurances from the IDF to assist in evacuations, the [[Gaza Health Ministry]] reported a lack of evacuation mechanisms, resulting in the deaths of several infants.<ref name="washingtonpost.com"/><ref name="aje.io"/><ref>{{cite news |last1=Yee |first1=Vivian |title=Premature Babies Are Evacuated From Embattled Hospital in Gaza |work=[[The New York Times]] |date=19 November 2023 |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/11/19/world/middleeast/premature-babies-al-shifa-hospital-gaza-evacuation.html#:~:text=Since%20Nov.%2011%2C%20at%20least,for%20more%20than%20a%20week. |access-date=19 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240128190938/https://www.nytimes.com/2023/11/19/world/middleeast/premature-babies-al-shifa-hospital-gaza-evacuation.html |archive-date=28 January 2024}}</ref>

The situation escalated in mid-November when Israel launched a [[Al-Shifa Hospital siege|raid on al-Shifa Hospital]].<ref name="The New York Times"/><ref name="Israel's claims of providing incuba"/> Evacuations eventually occurred, facilitated by the [[Palestinian Red Crescent]], [[World Health Organization]], and [[UNOCHA]], with 31 premature babies moved to southern Gaza, with most then to Egypt.<ref>{{cite news |date=20 November 2023 |title=Palestinian Red Crescent, UN agencies evacuate Al Shifa premature babies |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/palestinian-red-crescent-un-agencies-evacuate-al-shifa-premature-babies-2023-11-19/ |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=19 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231130043741/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/palestinian-red-crescent-un-agencies-evacuate-al-shifa-premature-babies-2023-11-19/ |archive-date=30 == Reactions ==
A variety of experts, organizations, and countries have labelled Israel's actions against Gaza as [[Gaza genocide|genocidal]],<ref>{{cite journal |last1=Shaw |first1=Martin |author-link=Martin Shaw (sociologist) |title=Inescapably Genocidal |journal=[[Journal of Genocide Research]] |date=3 January 2024 |pages=1–5 |doi=10.1080/14623528.2023.2300555 |s2cid=266778978}}</ref><ref>{{cite journal |last1=Levene |first1=Mark |author1-link=Mark Levene |title=Gaza 2023: Words Matter, Lives Matter More |journal=[[Journal of Genocide Research]] |date=21 January 2024 |pages=1–7 |doi=10.1080/14623528.2024.2301866}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=South Africa's ICJ Case Against Israel Backed by Over 1,000 Organizations |work=The Palestine Chronicle |date=10 January 2024 |url=https://www.palestinechronicle.com/south-africas-icj-case-against-israel-backed-by-over-1000-organizations/ |access-date=13 January 2024 |archive-date=12 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240112210235/https://www.palestinechronicle.com/south-africas-icj-case-against-israel-backed-by-over-1000-organizations/ |url-status=live}}</ref> using a variety of aspects of the humanitarian crisis as evidence.<ref name="HRW Blockade">{{cite web |date=26 February 2024 |title=Israel Not Complying with World Court Order in Genocide Case |url=https://www.hrw.org/news/2024/02/26/israel-not-complying-world-court-order-genocide-case |website=[[Human Rights Watch]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240227022141/https://www.hrw.org/news/2024/02/26/israel-not-complying-world-court-order-genocide-case |archive-date=27 February 2024}}</ref><ref ===Aid organizations===
A [[Doctors Without Borders]] video shared by [[Amnesty International]] head [[Agnès Callamard]] stated, "This brutal annihilation of an entire populations health system stretches beyond what humanitarian aid can fix."<ref>{{Cite tweet |user=AgnesCallamard |number=1727821600496537942 |title=This brutal annihilation of an entire population's health system stretches beyond what humanitarian aid can fix. Doctors can't stop bombs.}}</ref> On 4 December, [[Red Cross]] president [[Mirjana Spoljaric Egger]] visited the Gaza Strip, stating, "the things I saw there are beyond anything that anyone should be in a position to describe."<ref>{{cite web |date=4 December 2023 |title=Red Cross Chief Arrives In Gaza, Calls For Political Solution |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/red-cross-chief-arrives-in-gaza-calls-for-political-solution-451d4b7c |website=[[Barron's]] |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]] |access-date=5 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240205082644/https://www.barrons.com/news/red-cross-chief-arrives-in-gaza-calls-for-political-solution-451d4b7c |archive-date=5 February 2024}}</ref> On 10 December, Bushra Khalidi, an expert with [[Oxfam]], stated the situation was no longer "just a catastrophe, it's apocalyptic."<ref>{{cite news |title=Israeli forces battle Palestinian militants in south Gaza |url=https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20231210-israeli-forces-push-into-southern-gaza |work=[[France 24]] |date=10 December 2023 |access-date=10 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240118192752/https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20231210-israeli-forces-push-into-southern-gaza |archive-date=18 January 2024}}</ref>

On 11 December, the presidents of six major humanitarian organizations — [[CARE USA]], [[Mercy Corps]], the [[Norwegian Refugee Council]], [[Oxfam America]], [[Refugees International]], and [[Save the Children]] — penned a joint op-ed in ''[[The New York Times]]'' in which they stated, "We have seen nothing like the siege of Gaza".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Nunn |first1=Michelle |last2=D’Oyen McKenna |first2=Tjada |last3=Egeland |first3=Jan |last4=Maxman |first4=Abby |last5=Soeripto |first5=Janti |last6=Konyndyk |first6=Jeremy |title=We Are No Strangers to Human Suffering, but We've Seen Nothing |archive-date=22 December 2023}}</ref> On 13 December, a group of Israeli human rights and civil society organizations, including [[B'Tselem]], penned an open-letter to [[Joe Biden]] urging him to use In response to a week-long [[communications blackout]] across Gaza in January 2024, the non-profit [[Access Now]] stated, "It is unconscionable to toy with connectivity amidst unprecedented violence and unfathomable human suffering."<ref>{{cite web |title=A week in the dark: connectivity in Gaza must be restored now |url=https://www.accessnow.org/press-release/gaza-a-week-in-the-dark/ |website=Access Now |access-date=19 January 2024}}</ref> On 9 February, an [[International Rescue Committee]] representative stated, "If they aren’t killed in the fighting, Palestinian children, women and men will be at risk of dying by starvation or disease."<ref>{{cite news |date=9 February 2024 |title=If attacks don't kill Gaza's people, starvation and disease will: Aid group |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/2/9/israels-war-on-gaza-live-fear-in-rafah-as-israel-prepares-ground-attack?update=2694509 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=11 February 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240718082450/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/2/9/israels-war-on-gaza-live-fear-in-rafah-as-israel-prepares-ground-attack?update=2694509 |archive-date=18 July 2024}}</ref> On 18 February, the heads of eight major humanitarian organizations wrote a joint op-ed, stating, "The speed of the deterioration in Gaza is unprecedented in recent history."<ref>{{cite web |last1=Callahan |first1=Sean |last2=Egeland |first2=Jan |last3=D’Oyen McKenna |first3=Tjada |last4=Konyndyk |first4=Jeremy |last5=Maxman |first5=Abby |last6=Nunn |first6=Michelle |last7=Soeripto |first7=Janti |last8=Owubah |first8=Charles |title=Palestinians in Gaza face mass starvation. |archive-date=17 August 2024}}</ref> [[Civicus]] described the situation as "one of the worst humanitarian crises in recent global history".<ref>{{cite news |first1=Federica |last1=Marsi |first2=Edna |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/3/5/israels-war-on-gaza-live-israeli-attacks-on-aid-seekers-continue?update=2749557 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=8 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240308050254/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/3/5/israels-war-on-gaza-live-israeli-attacks-on-aid-seekers-continue?update=2749557 |archive-date=8 March 2024}}</ref> Agnès Callamard, the head of Amnesty, stated, "While the international community is busy pretending Gaza is a humanitarian crisis, Israel continues to violate international law in total impunity".<ref>{{cite news |first=Usaid |last=Siddiqui |date=14 March 2024 |title=While the international community is busy pretending Gaza is a humanitarian crisis, Israel continues to violate international law in total impunity |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/3/14/israels-war-on-gaza-live-rafah-attack-coming-soon-despite-pressure?update=2771334 |work=[[Al Jazeera |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240817180350/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/3/14/israels-war-on-gaza-live-rafah-attack-coming-soon-despite-pressure?update=2771334 |archive-date=17 August 2024}}</ref>

The British medical journal ''[[The Lancet]]'' issued a warning that the actual death toll in Gaza from both direct and indirect causes could be more than 186,000.<ref>{{cite journal |last1=Khatib |first1=Rasha |last2=McKee |first2=Martin |author2-link=Martin McKee |last3=Yusuf |first3=Salim |author3-link=Salim Yusuf |title=Counting the dead in Gaza: difficult but essential |journal=[[The Lancet]] |publisher=Elsevier BV |date=5 July 2024 |volume=404 |issue=10449 |pages=237–238 |issn=0140-6736 |doi=10.1016/s0140-6736(24)01169-3 |pmid=38976995 |url=https://www.thelancet.com/journals/lancet/article/PIIS0140-6736(24)01169-3/fulltext |quote=Applying a conservative estimate of four indirect deaths per one direct death to the 37,396 deaths reported, it is not implausible to estimate that up to 186,000 or even more deaths could be attributable to the current conflict in Gaza.}}</ref> Jean-François Corty, a humanitarian doctor and president of the NGO ''[[Médecins du Monde|Doctors of the World]]'', said that the Gaza Health Ministry's figures take into account the identified dead, "without taking into account all the dead left under the rubble of the bombardments, or the indirect victims who died because of a lack of care or [[Health care|access to care]], or from being transported to a health centre. If you add those who are likely to die of [[malnutrition]] or as a result of [[wound]]s inflicted by Israeli bombardments in the weeks and months to come, because of the risks of [[superinfection]] and because their pathology will be treated late, then yes, the figure of 186,000 deaths mentioned in The Lancet is credible."<ref>{{cite news |first=Marc |last=Daou |title='More than 186,000 dead' in Gaza: How credible are the estimates published on The Lancet? |url=https://www.france24.com/en/middle-east/20240711-more-than-186-000-dead-in-gaza-how-credible-are-the-estimates-published-on-the-lancet |work=[[France 24]] |date=11 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240815183540/https://www.france24.com/en/middle-east/20240711-more-than-186-000-dead-in-gaza-how-credible-are-the-estimates-published-on-the-lancet |archive-date=15 August 2024}}</ref>

==== United Nations ====
[[File:OSN 2023.png|thumb|On 27 October, the [[United Nations General Assembly]] passed [[United Nations General Assembly Resolution ES-10/21|Resolution ES-10/21 calling for]] an "immediate and sustained" humanitarian truce and cessation of hostilities.]]
[[UNRWA]] commissioner [[Philippe Lazzarini]] described the situation as "bone-chilling," and the [[World Health Organization]] stated that it was "spiraling out of control."<ref name="Residents flee Gaza City">{{cite news |last1=Reed |first1=John |last2=Mehul |first2=Srivastava |date=13 October 2023 |title=Residents flee Gaza City as Israel tells 1.1mn to leave |work=[[Financial Times]] |url=https://www.ft.com/content/8ea2374e-c21c-4232-bc69-615e36b26caa?shareType=nongift |url-access=subscription |access-date=13 October 2023 |archive-date=13 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231013184255/https://www.ft.com/content/8ea2374e-c21c-4232-bc69-615e36b26caa?shareType=nongift |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="aj-hosp">{{cite news |date=17 October 2023 |title=Israel-Hamas war live: Biden in Israel, anger over Gaza hospital attack |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/10/17/israel-hamas-war-live-anger-after-israeli-strike-kills-500-in-hospital |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=18 October 2023 |archive-date=18 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231018043239/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/10/17/israel-hamas-war-live-anger-after-israeli-strike-kills-500-in-hospital |url-status=live}}</ref> On October 26, the World Organization declared that Gaza's humanitarian and health crisis had "reached catastrophic proportions."<ref>{{cite tweet |user=WHOEMRO |number=1717555357864677477 |date=26 October 2023 |title='The humanitarian and health crisis in Gaza has reached catastrophic proportions. It is our moral duty, an imperative that transcends political boundaries, to demand unobstructed access for delivering life-saving aid.' – Dr Ahmed Al-Mandhari, @WHOEMRO Regional Director |author=WHO Regional Office for the Eastern Mediterranean |access-date=26 October 2023}}</ref> [[Martin Griffiths]], the United Nations head of Humanitarian Affairs, stated the humanitarian crisis in Gaza was the worst he had ever seen in his life, stating, "I don’t say that lightly. I mean, I started off in my 20s dealing with the [[Khmer Rouge]], and you remember how bad that was, the [[Killing Fields|killing fields]]."<ref>{{cite news |last1=Amanpour |first1=Christiane |title=UN calls for ceasefire but would welcome shorter pause to get more aid into Gaza, relief chief says |url=https://www.cnn.com/middleeast/live-news/israel-hamas-war-gaza-news-11-21-23/h_a534998db297fdd1e6dd543f1e4dfc4f |work=[[CNN]] |date=21 November 2023 |access-date=23 November 2023}}</ref> Griffith stated it was the worst ever because unlike in other humanitarian crises, the people of Gaza had nowhere to flee.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Mance |first1=Henry |date= |title=UN aid chief Martin Griffiths: 'The war in Gaza isn't halfway through' |url=https://www.ft.com/content/01b592be-47c7-4a20-9bbd-621aa40f7640?shareType=nongift |work=[[Financial Times]] |access-date=18 December 2023 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20231218055845/https://www.ft.com/content/01b592be-47c7-4a20-9bbd-621aa40f7640 |archive-date=18 December 2023}}</ref> On November 8, UN Human Rights chief [[Volker Türk]] described the [[Rafah Crossing]] as "gates to a living nightmare."<ref>{{cite news |first1=Joseph |last1=Stepansky |first2=Farah |last2=Najjar |date=8 November 2023 |title='We have fallen off a precipice', UN human rights chief says |url=https://aje.io/d5kugr?update=2472540 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=8 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231121141705/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/11/8/israel-hamas-war-live-humanitarian-aid-targeted-amid-gaza-bombardment?update=2472540 |archive-date=21 November 2023}}</ref>

On 28 November, UN chief [[António Guterres]] stated, the "humanitarian catastrophe in Gaza is getting worse by the day."<ref>{{cite news |title=UN Chief Pushes for Gaza Truce to Become Full Humanitarian Cease-fire |url=https://www.voanews.com/a/7372505.html |work=[[VOA]] |date=27 November 2023 |agency=[[Reuters]] |access-date=29 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240222171337/https://www.voanews.com/a/7372505.html |archive-date=22 February 2024}}</ref> On 3 December, WHO secretary-general [[Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus]] visited [[Nasser Medical Complex]], stating, "Patients were receiving care on the floor, screaming in pain... I cannot find words strong enough to express our concern over what we’re witnessing."<ref>{{cite news |first1=Virginia |last1=Pietromarchi |first2=Stephen |last2=Quillen |date=3 December 2023 |title=Gaza hospital conditions 'unimaginable', WHO says |url=https://aje.io/h1s5og?update=2530674 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=3 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231217222954/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/12/3/israel-gaza-war-live-israel-bombards-gaza-as-talks-break-down?update=2530674 |archive-date=17 December 2023}}</ref> On 6 December, UN chief António Guterres invoked Article 99 of the [[Charter of the United Nations]], stating “We are facing a severe risk of collapse of the humanitarian system."<ref>{{cite news |last1=Shotter |first1=James |last2=Saleh |first2=Heba |date=6 December 2023 |title=Humanitarian system in Gaza on verge of collapse, says UN chief |url=https://www.ft.com/content/752eb5a0-3d75-4340-ad0d-b6554d9e4f61 |work=[[Financial Times]] |access-date=7 December 2023 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20231206203515/https://www.ft.com/content/752eb5a0-3d75-4340-ad0d-b6554d9e4f61 |archive-date=6 December 2023}}</ref> A joint statement by more than 20 UN and humanitarian organizations described the crisis as "amongst the worst we have witnessed".<ref>{{cite web |title=Aqaba Process Joint Statement on Gaza's Humanitarian Situation |url=https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/aqaba-process-joint-statement-gazas-humanitarian-situation |website=[[ReliefWeb]] |date=6 December 2023 |publisher=[[UNOCHA]] |access-date=8 December 2023 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240811200221/https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/aqaba-process-joint-statement-gazas-humanitarian-situation-enar |archive-date=11 August 2024}}</ref>
