On 7 January, UN chief Antonio Guterres stated "widespread famine looms" in Gaza,<ref>{{cite news |last1=Andres |first1=Paula |title=Israeli strikes kill 7 civilians in West Bank, 2 journalists in Gaza |url=https://www.politico.eu/article/israel-west-bank-journalists-gaza-hamas/#:~:text=Adding%20to%20a%20growing%20death,Security%20Council%20members%20Friday%20evening. |work=[[Politico]] |date=7 January 2024 |access-date=8 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240226092407/https://www.politico.eu/article/israel-west-bank-journalists-gaza-hamas/ |archive-date=26 February 2024}}</ref> to which the UN special rapporteur for health [[Tlaleng Mofokeng]] stated Gaza was experiencing "deliberate starvation not famine".<ref>{{cite news |first1=Lyndal |last1=Rowlands |date=7 January 2024 |title='Deliberate starvation not famine': UN human rights expert |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/7/israel-war-on-gaza-live-signs-of-starvation-everywhere-in-southern-gaza?update=2601737 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=8 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240107012821/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/7/israel-war-on-gaza-live-signs-of-starvation-everywhere-in-southern-gaza?update=2601737 |archive-date=7 January 2024}}</ref> Speaking at the [[United Nations Security Council]] on 12 January, Martin Griffiths stated colleagues who had made it into northern Gaza in recent days had described "scenes of utter horror: Corpses left lying in the road. People with evident signs of starvation stopping trucks in search of anything they can get to survive."<ref>{{cite web |title=Mr. Martin Griffiths, Under-Secretary-General for Humanitarian Affairs and Emergency Relief Coordinator - Briefing to the UN Security Council on the humanitarian situation in Israel and the Occupied Palestinian Territory, 12 January 2024 |url=https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/mr-martin-griffiths-under-secretary-general-humanitarian-affairs-and-emergency-relief-coordinator-briefing-un-security-council-humanitarian-situation-israel-and-occupied-palestinian-territory-12-january-2024 |website=[[ReliefWeb]] |date=12 January 2024 |publisher=[[UNOCHA]] |access-date=13 January 2024 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240825161328/https://reliefweb.int/report/occupied-palestinian-territory/mr-martin-griffiths-under-secretary-general-humanitarian-affairs-and-emergency-relief-coordinator-briefing-un-security-council-humanitarian-situation-israel-and-occupied-palestinian-territory-12-january-2024-enhe |archive-date=25 August 2024}}</ref> The [[World Food Programme]] stated nine out of ten people in northern Gaza were eating less than a meal a day.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Cameron |first1=David |author-link=David Cameron |title=Israel must act now to let aid through and save lives in Gaza. On 20 January, Antonio Guterres stated, "People in Gaza are dying not only from bombs and bullets, but from lack of food & clean water, and hospitals without power & medicine."<ref>{{cite news |title=Guterres cataloga de "inaceptable" la negativa israelí de admitir un Estado palestino |language=es |trans-title=Guterres calls Israel's refusal to admit a Palestinian state "unacceptable" |url=https://www.france24.com/es/medio-oriente/20240120-guterres-cataloga-de-inaceptable-la-negativa-israelí-de-admitir-un-estado-palestino |work=[[France24]] |date=20 January 2024 |access-date=21 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240219080902/https://www.france24.com/es/medio-oriente/20240120-guterres-cataloga-de-inaceptable-la-negativa-israel%C3%AD-de-admitir-un-estado-palestino |archive-date=19 February 2024}}</ref> On 27 January, Martin Griffiths stated, "The people of Gaza have been enduring unthinkable horrors and deprivation for close to four months. Their needs have never been higher."<ref>{{cite news |title=UN humanitarian chief says it is 'not the time' to deprive people in Gaza of assistance |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/27/israels-war-on-gaza-live-hospital-blackout-amid-khan-younis-assault?update=2653822 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=28 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240128015258/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/27/israels-war-on-gaza-live-hospital-blackout-amid-khan-younis-assault?update=2653822 |archive-date=28 January 2024}}</ref> On 30 January, the [[UN Security Council]] issued a statement saying it was worried about the "dire and rapidly deteriorating humanitarian situation".<ref>{{cite news |title=UN Security Council says worried by 'dire and rapidly deteriorating' conditions in Gaza |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/un-security-council-says-worried-by-dire-and-rapidly-deteriorating-conditions-in-gaza/ |work=[[Times of Israel]] |agency=[[Reuters]] |access-date=31 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240131042929/https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/un-security-council-says-worried-by-dire-and-rapidly-deteriorating-conditions-in-gaza/ |archive-date=31 January 2024}}</ref> On 7 February, Martin Griffiths stated, "More than half of Gaza’s population is now crammed in Rafah, a town of originally 250,000 people right on Egypt’s doorstep. Their living conditions are abysmal – they lack the basic necessities to survive, stalked by hunger, disease and death."<ref>{{cite web |last1=Griffith |first1=Martin |title=UN relief chief: As crisis enters fifth month, further fighting in Rafah risks claiming more lives and exacerbating humanitarian needs |url=https://www.unocha.org/news/un-relief-chief-crisis-enters-fifth-month-further-fighting-rafah-risks-claiming-more-lives-and#:~:text=More%20than%20half%20of%20Gaza%27s,by%20hunger%2C%20disease%20and%20death. |website=[[OCHA]] |publisher=[[United Nations]] |access-date=8 February 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240221221146/https://www.unocha.org/news/un-relief-chief-crisis-enters-fifth-month-further-fighting-rafah-risks-claiming-more-lives-and |archive-date=21 February 2024}}</ref> On 10 February, António Guterres stated an Israeli assault on [[Rafah]] would "exponentially increase what is already a humanitarian nightmare".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Zaanoun |first1=Adel |title=Strikes On Gaza's Rafah As US Warns Of Potential 'Disaster' |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/strikes-on-gaza-s-rafah-as-us-warns-of-potential-disaster-077b447d |magazine=[[Barron's]] |access-date=11 February 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240219080903/https://www.barrons.com/news/strikes-on-gaza-s-rafah-as-us-warns-of-potential-disaster-077b447d |archive-date=19 February 2024}}</ref> On 21 February, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus stated the situation in Gaza was inhumane and described it as a death zone.<ref>{{cite news |date=21 February 2024 |title=Gaza Humanitarian Situation 'Inhumane': WHO |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/gaza-humanitarian-situation-inhumane-who-2c97d982 |magazine=[[Barron's]] |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]] |access-date=22 February 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240222044618/https://www.barrons.com/news/gaza-humanitarian-situation-inhumane-who-2c97d982 |archive-date=22 February 2024}}</ref>

On 5 March, UNRWA chief Philippe Lazzarini stated, "Despite all the horrors that Gazans have lived through – and that we have watched – the worst might be yet to come."<ref>{{cite news |last1=Butler |first1=Josh |title=Australia urges Israel to provide evidence for allegations UNRWA staff were involved in 7 October attacks |url=https://www.theguardian.com/australia-news/2024/mar/05/unrwa-funding-pause-australia-urges-israel-evidence-allegations-hamas-7-october-attack |work=[[The Guardian]] |date=5 March 2024 |archive-date=6 April 2024}}</ref> On 15 March, a representative from the United Nations Population Fund called the humanitarian crisis in northern Gaza a "nightmare".<ref>{{cite news |title=In Gaza, there are no more 'normal-sized babies': UN official |url=https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20240315-in-gaza-there-are-no-more-normal-sized-babies-un-official |work=[[France24]] |date=15 March Guterres stated the situation in Gaza was a "non-stop nightmare. Communities obliterated. Homes demolished. Entire families and generations wiped out."<ref>{{cite news |title=End War's 'Nightmare', UN Chief Says At Gates Of Gaza |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/end-non-stop-nightmare-un-chief-says-at-gates-of-gaza-d8bb5752 |work=[[Barron's]] |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]] |access-date=25 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240325232405/https://www.barrons.com/news/end-non-stop-nightmare-un-chief-says-at-gates-of-gaza-d8bb5752 |archive-date=25 March 2024}}</ref>

===Israeli===
Israeli Major General (ret.) [[Giora Eiland]] compared Israel's situation to that of the United States after [[Pearl Harbor]].<ref name="Eiland 2023-10-10" /> He argued that if Israel wanted to disarm Hamas, it had "no choice" but to make Gaza a place "that is temporarily or permanently impossible to live in".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Khalidi |first1=Rashid |title=The U.S. Should Think Twice About Israel's Plans for Gaza |work=[[The New York Times]] |date=15 October 2023 |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/10/15/opinion/israel-united-states-gaza.html |access-date=26 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240708154634/https://www.nytimes.com/2023/10/15/opinion/israel-united-states-gaza.html |archive-date=8 July 2024}}</ref><ref name="Eiland 2023-10-10">{{Cite news |last=איילנד |first=גיורא |date=10 October 2023 |title=זו לא נקמה. זה או אנחנו או הם |trans-title=This is not revenge. It's either us or them |language=he |work=[[Ynet]] |url=https://www.ynet.co.il/yedioth/article/yokra13625377 |access-date=3 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240529060225/https://www.ynet.co.il/yedioth/article/yokra13625377 |archive-date=29 May 2024}}</ref> This, he stated, was not a "program for revenge", but a way to get the hostages back.<ref>{{cite news |last=Whitman |first=Ariel |date=10 August 2023 |title=Giora Eiland outlines plan to get hostages back alive |language=en |work=Globes |url=https://en.globes.co.il/en/article-giora-eiland-outlines-plan-to-get-hostages-back-alive-1001459631 |access-date=3 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240414090150/https://en.globes.co.il/en/article-giora-eiland-outlines-plan-to-get-hostages-back-alive-1001459631 |archive-date=14 April 2024}}</ref> In an op-ed in ''[[Yedioth Ahronoth]]'' on 19 November, Eiland wrote Israel should not adopt a US narrative that "allows" Israel to only fight against militants.<ref>{{cite news |last1=McKernan |first1=Bethan |title=Gaza's main hospital has become a 'death zone', says WHO |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/nov/19/gazas-main-hospital-has-become-a-death-zone-says-who |work=[[The |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240522195131/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/nov/19/gazas-main-hospital-has-become-a-death-zone-says-who |archive-date=22 May 2024}}</ref> Writing for ''[[Haaretz]]'', Zvi Bar'el argued the humanitarian crisis was an Israeli military weapon that could be used as a bargaining chip.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Bar'el |first1=Zvi |title=Gaza's Humanitarian Crisis Turns Into a Strategic Weapon for Israel |access-date=20 November 2023 |archive-date=11 November 2023}}</ref> In a speech posted by the ''[[Knesset Channel]]'', MK [[Tally Gotliv]] stated, "Without hunger and thirst among the Gazan population, we will not be able to recruit collaborators".<ref>{{Cite tweet |user=KnessetT |number=1716502486331113922 |title="בלי רעב וצמא אצל האוכלוסייה העזתית לא נצליח לגייס משת"פ, לא נצליח לגייס מודיעין, לא נצליח לשחד אנשים, באוכל, בשתייה, בתרופות, כדי להשיג מודיעין ואנחנו יודעים שמציאת החטופים היא מטרה עליונה וסופר חשובה לצד מטרות הלחימה." - כך אמרה ח"כ טלי גוטליב במליאת הכנסת |language=he |trans-title=}}</ref>

[[Ghassan Alian]], the head of [[Coordinator of Government Activities in the Territories|COGAT]], stated, "Human animals are dealt with accordingly. Israel has imposed a total blockade on Gaza, no electricity, no water, just damage. You wanted hell, you will get hell."<ref>{{cite news |last1=Jones |first1=Owen |title=The brutality and inhumanity of Israel's assault on Gaza is no surprise. It's just what was promised |url=https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2024/jan/13/israel-hamas-gaza-war-crimes |work=[[The Guardian]] |date=13 January 2024 |access-date=22 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240528222143/https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2024/jan/13/israel-hamas-gaza-war-crimes |archive-date=28 May 2024}}</ref> In January 2024, a COGAT representative denied there was a famine in Gaza, stating, "Don't forget that this is an Arab, Gazan population whose DNA is to hoard, certainly when it comes to food."<ref>{{cite news |last1=Gontarz |first1=Nir |date=12 January 2024 |title=Half a Million Gazans Are Suffering From Acute Hunger. Let That Sink In |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2024-01-12/ty-article-magazine/.highlight/half-a-million-gazans-are-suffering-from-acute-hunger-let-that-sink-in/0000018c-fd57-d517-af9d-fd7f19b10000 |work=[[Haaretz]] |access-date=15 January 2024 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240311143325/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2024-01-12/ty-article-magazine/.highlight/half-a-million-gazans-are-suffering-from-acute-hunger-let-that-sink-in/0000018c-fd57-d517-af9d-fd7f19b10000 |archive-date=11 March 2024}}</ref> Netanyahu stated Israel was allowing in the absolute "minimum" amount of aid into Gaza and claimed this was preventing a humanitarian crisis.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Berman |first1=Lazar |date= |title=Netanyahu: We're allowing 'minimum' amount of aid necessary in order to prevent Gaza humanitarian crisis |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/netanyahu-were-allowing-minimum-amount-of-aid-necessary-in-order-to-prevent-gaza-humanitarian-crisis/#:~:text=January%2018%2C%202024-,Netanyahu%3A%20We%27re%20allowing%20%27minimum%27%20amount%20of%20aid,to%20prevent%20Gaza%20humanitarian%20crisis&text=Answering%20a%20question%20about%20humanitarian,to%20prevent%20a%20humanitarian%20crisis. |work=[[Times of Israel]] |access-date=22 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240529080153/https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/netanyahu-were-allowing-minimum-amount-of-aid-necessary-in-order-to-prevent-gaza-humanitarian-crisis/ |archive-date=29 May 2024}}</ref>

=== Palestinian ===
On 4 January 2024, Gaza City mayor [[Yahya Al-Sarraj]] made an urgent appeal to the international community for fuel "to provide the necessary support mechanisms to provide water, sanitation and hygiene services to serve all residents of the Gaza Strip".<ref>{{cite news |first1=Ali |last1=Harb |first2=Brian |last2=Osgood |date=4 January 2024 |title=Gaza's mayor issues urgent global appeal for fuel supplies |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/4/israel-hamas-war-live-bloody-day-for-hezbollah-tensions-with-israel-soar?update=2597271 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=5 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240105034901/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/4/israel-hamas-war-live-bloody-day-for-hezbollah-tensions-with-israel-soar?update=2597271 |archive-date=5 January 2024}}</ref> On 5 January, the [[Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Expatriates (State of Palestine)|Palestinian Foreign Ministry]] stated the humanitarian crisis in Rafah was straining the international community's credibility, stating, "The Israeli government continues its deepening campaign of genocide, comprehensive destruction, and displacement in the Gaza Strip".<ref>{{cite news |first1=Brian |last1=Osgood |first2=Adam |last2=Muro |date=5 January 2024 |title=Palestinian Foreign Ministry: Humanitarian crisis in Rafah tests international community's |archive-date=5 January 2024}}</ref> On 14 January, the Foreign Ministry stated, "The Israeli occupation has turned Gaza into an uninhabitable place, committed horrific crimes, and forcibly displaced approximately 2 million people".<ref>{{cite news |first=Joseph |last=Stepansky |date=14 January 2024 |title='Hundred days of genocide in Gaza is lifetime of pain': Palestinian foreign ministry |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/1/14/israels-war-on-gaza-live-100-days-of-war-in-gaza-as-more-children-killed?update=2619645 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=15 |archive-date=25 August 2024}}</ref>

=== United States ===

Ten days into the war, the United States UN representative [[Linda Thomas-Greenfield]] vetoed a [[UN Security Council]] resolution that would have condemned all violence against civilians in the war and urged humanitarian aid to Gaza. She said it was too early to craft a resolution while diplomacy was underway and criticized the one proposed for not mentioning Israel's right to self-defense.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Lederer |first1=Edith |title=US vetoes UN resolution condemning Hamas' attacks on Israel and all violence against civilians |url=https://apnews.com/article/un-security-council-resolution-gaza-hamas-1c23913f8552f5379b2c158a83493835 |work=[[Associated Press]] |date=18 October 2023 |access-date=18 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240801081738/https://apnews.com/article/un-security-council-resolution-gaza-hamas-1c23913f8552f5379b2c158a83493835 |archive-date=1 August 2024}}</ref> In a ''[[Wall Street Journal]]'' op-ed, conservative American commentator [[Daniel Henninger]] speculated Hamas wanted to create a humanitarian crisis for publicity purposes.<ref>{{cite news |last=Henninger |first=Daniel |date=15 November 2023 |title=Gaza Is the First Humanitarian-Crisis War |url=https://www.wsj.com/articles/the-first-humanitarian-crisis-war-israel-al-shifa-hospital-hamas-6c108eee |work=[[The Wall Street Journal]] |access-date=20 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240515135332/https://www.wsj.com/articles/the-first-humanitarian-crisis-war-israel-al-shifa-hospital-hamas-6c108eee |archive-date=15 May 2024}}</ref>

US Vice-President [[Kamala Harris]] said on 2 December that "too many innocent Palestinians have been killed" and that "international humanitarian law must be respected". She said that at the end of the conflict there must be "No forcible displacement, no reoccupation, no siege or blockade, no reduction in territory, and no use of Gaza as a platform for terrorism".<ref>{{cite news |first=Josh |last=Meyer |title=VP Harris calls on Israel to respect international law, stop killing innocent Palestinians |url=https://eu.usatoday.com/story/news/world/israel-hamas/2023/12/02/kamala-harris-rebuke-israel-gaza-killings/71783397007/ |work=[[USA Today]] |date=2 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240328163553/https://www.usatoday.com/story/news/world/israel-hamas/2023/12/02/kamala-harris-rebuke-israel-gaza-killings/71783397007/ |archive-date=28 March 2024}}</ref> Ten days later, US President Biden warned that Israel was losing international support because of its "indiscriminate bombing" of Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |first1=Colleen |last1=Long |first2=Aamer |last2=Madhani |title=Biden takes a tougher stance on Israel's 'indiscriminate bombing' of Gaza |url=https://apnews.com/article/biden-israel-hamas-oct-7-44c4229d4c1270d9cfa484b664a22071 |work=[[Associated Press]] |date=12 December 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240816080939/https://apnews.com/article/biden-israel-hamas-oct-7-44c4229d4c1270d9cfa484b664a22071 |archive-date=16 August 2024}}</ref>

In early March 2024, the United States began [[airdrops]] of humanitarian aid into Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Ryan |first1=Missy |last2=DeYoung |first2=Karen |last3=Abutaleb |first3=Yasmeen |last4=Lamothe |first4=Dan |title=As Gaza crisis intensifies, U.S. conducts first airdrop of aid |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2024/03/02/airdrop-gaza-food-military/ |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]] |access-date=3 March 2024 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240302235748/https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2024/03/02/airdrop-gaza-food-military/ |archive-date=2 March 2024}}</ref> Following an incident in which an airdrop of aid killed 5 Gazans and injured several others, the [[US Central Command]]<ref>{{cite news |last1=Imane Kouachi |first1=Ikrame |title=US denies its plane involved in airdrop aid incident in Gaza, resulting in 5 Palestinians' deaths |url=https://www.aa.com.tr/en/world/us-denies-its-plane-involved-in-airdrop-aid-incident-in-gaza-resulting-in-5-palestinians-deaths/3159930 |work=[[Anadolu Agency]] |date=9 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240804085402/https://www.aa.com.tr/en/world/us-denies-its-plane-involved-in-airdrop-aid-incident-in-gaza-resulting-in-5-palestinians-deaths/3159930 |archive-date=4 August 2024}}</ref> and an unnamed U.S. official on 8 March rejected reports that their airdrops were to blame.<ref>{{cite news |date=8 March 2024 |title=Israel-Hamas war: U.S. official rejects claims that U.S. airdrop killed civilians |url=https://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/live-blog/israel-hamas-war-live-updates-rcna142399 |work=[[NBC News]] |access-date=4 August 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240528070617/https://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/live-blog/israel-hamas-war-live-updates-rcna142399 |archive-date=28 May 2024}}</ref> The US also began work on opening a 'maritime aid corridor' and building the [[Gaza floating pier]] so aid could be delivered by sea.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Horton |first1=Alex |title=How the U.S. military will use a floating pier to deliver Gaza aid |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2024/03/08/gaza-floating-pier/ |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]] |access-date=10 March 2024 |archive-date=9 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240309022530/https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2024/03/08/gaza-floating-pier/ |url-status=live}}</ref> On 4 March, US Vice-President Harris called for "an immediate ceasefire" because of "the immense scale of suffering in Gaza". She said Israel must let more aid into Gaza and was imposing "unnecessary restrictions".<ref>{{cite web |date=4 March 2024 |title=US VP Harris calls for 'immediate' Gaza truce in rare rebuke of Israel |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/3/4/us-vp-harris-calls-for-immediate-gaza-ceasefire-in-rare-rebuke-of-israel |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=4 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240819100536/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/3/4/us-vp-harris-calls-for-immediate-gaza-ceasefire-in-rare-rebuke-of-israel |archive-date=19 August 2024}}</ref> US Senator [[Chris Van Hollen]] had said that "political decisions by the Netanyahu coalition" were delaying the delivery of aid into Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Nazarro |first1=Miranda |title=Van Hollen agrees Israel should face 'consequences' over Gaza aid, civilian deaths |url=https://thehill.com/policy/international/4394248-van-hollen-agrees-israel-should-face-consequences-over-gaza-aid-civilian-deaths/#:~:text=“There%20are%20two%20big%20things,Netanyahu%20coalition%2C”%20he%20said. |work=[[The Hill (newspaper)|The Hill]] |date=7 January 2024 |access-date=8 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240126091102/https://thehill.com/policy/international/4394248-van-hollen-agrees-israel-should-face-consequences-over-gaza-aid-civilian-deaths/ |archive-date=26 January 2024}}</ref>

The US put forward a draft UN Security Council resolution which stated the "imperative" for "an immediate and sustained ceasefire", facilitating aid delivery, and supporting ongoing talks between Israel and Hamas, linked to the release of hostages. On 22 March it was vetoed by Russia and China.<ref>{{cite web |title=Russia and China veto US resolution stating imperative of 'immediate and sustained ceasefire' in Gaza |url=https://news.un.org/en/story/2024/03/1147856 |publisher=[[United Nations]] |date=22 March 2024}}</ref> On 25 March, the US abstained on a [[United Nations Security Council Resolution 2728|UN Security Council ceasefire resolution]], allowing it to pass.<ref>{{cite web |title=UN Security Council demands 'immediate ceasefire' in Gaza, ending months-long deadlock |url=https://news.un.org/en/story/2024/03/1147951 |website=UN News |publisher=[[United Nations]] |date=25 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240828203048/https://news.un.org/en/story/2024/03/1147951 |archive-date=28 August 2024}}</ref> On 26 March, the U.S. Secretary of Defense called the situation in Gaza a "human catastrophe".<ref>{{cite news |first1=Federica |last1=Marsi |first2=Usaid |last2=Siddiqui |date=26 March 2024 |title=Situation in Gaza a 'human catastrophe': Pentagon chief |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/3/26/israels-war-on-gaza-live-world-welcomes-un-ceasefire-resolution?update=2800277 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=29 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240831192544/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/3/26/israels-war-on-gaza-live-world-welcomes-un-ceasefire-resolution?update=2800277 |archive-date=31 August 2024}}</ref>

US [[Republican Party (United States)|Republican]] Congressman and former aide to [[Donald Trump]], [[Max Miller (politician)|Max Miller]], speaking at [[Fox News]] stated that Palestine is "about to get eviscerated... to turn that into a parking lot." He has previously called on the Biden administration "to get out of Israel's way and to let Israel do what it needs to do best". He said there should be "no rules of engagement" during Israel's bombardment of Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |date=26 October 2023 |title=US congressman: 'Palestine will be turned into a parking lot' |work=[[Middle East Monitor]] |url=https://www.middleeastmonitor.com/20231026-us-congressman-palestine-will-be-turned-into-a-parking-lot/ |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231028030424/https://www.middleeastmonitor.com/20231026-us-congressman-palestine-will-be-turned-into-a-parking-lot/ |archive-date=28 October 2023}}</ref> Miller also questioned the accuracy of the [[Gaza Health Ministry]]'s claim that 10,000 people have been killed in Gaza, saying that he believes many of those killed have been "Hamas terrorists", not innocent civilians, and said the United States does not "trust an entity that puts munitions in mosques, and churches and in hospitals."<ref>{{cite web |last=Eaton |first=Sabrina |date=17 November 2023 |title=U.S. Rep. Max Miller defends Israel's conduct of Hamas war after visit to Tel Aviv |url=https://www.cleveland.com/news/2023/11/us-rep-max-miller-defends-israels-conduct-of-hamas-war-after-visit-to-tel-aviv.html |access-date=3 December 2023 |website=cleveland.com |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231216072034/https://www.cleveland.com/news/2023/11/us-rep-max-miller-defends-israels-conduct-of-hamas-war-after-visit-to-tel-aviv.html |archive-date=16 December 2023}}</ref>

Former Republican [[United States House of Representatives|Representative]] [[Michele Bachmann]] appearing in December in [[Charlie Kirk|The Charlie Kirk Show]] stated "So, it's time that Gaza ends. The two million people who live there – they are clever assassins. They need to be removed from that land. That land needs to be turned into a national park. And since they're the voluntary mercenaries for Iran, they need to be dropped on the doorstep of Iran. Let Iran deal with those people." She received a round of applause from the audience, while Kirk replied "I look at Israel and Israel says we never want another person into our country that doesn't share our values," Kirk said. "They said they don't want refugees. They don't want any of these people. I want American immigration policy to be like that."<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 December 2023 |title=Michele Bachmann Calls for Ethnic Cleansing in Gaza: 'They Need To Be Removed From That Land' |url=https://www.mediaite.com/tv/michele-bachmann-calls-for-ethnic-cleansing-in-gaza-they-need-to-be-removed-from-that-land/ |access-date=19 December 2023 |website=[[Mediaite]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231224135124/https://www.mediaite.com/tv/michele-bachmann-calls-for-ethnic-cleansing-in-gaza-they-need-to-be-removed-from-that-land/ |archive-date=24 December 2023}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |author=Media Matters Staff |date=18 December 2023 |title=Michelle Bachmann to Charlie Kirk: "It's time that Gaza ends. The 2 million people who live there, they are clever assassins. They need to be removed from that land." |url=https://www.mediamatters.org/charlie-kirk/michelle-bachmann-charlie-kirk-its-time-gaza-ends-2-million-people-who-live-there-they |access-date=19 December 2023 |website=[[Media Matters for America]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231219113014/https://www.mediamatters.org/charlie-kirk/michelle-bachmann-charlie-kirk-its-time-gaza-ends-2-million-people-who-live-there-they |archive-date=19 December 2023}}</ref>

Republican Representative, [[Brian Mast]], compared all Palestinians to Nazis in November on the House floor.<ref>{{cite magazine |last=Otten |first=Tori |date=1 November 2023 |title=Republican Representative Directly Compares All Palestinians to Nazis |url=https://newrepublic.com/post/176559/republican-representative-brian-mast-compares-palestinians-nazis |access-date=3 February 2024 |magazine=[[The New Republic]] |issn=0028-6583 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240203033548/https://newrepublic.com/post/176559/republican-representative-brian-mast-compares-palestinians-nazis |archive-date=3 February 2024}}</ref> On January 31, 2024, Mast also said that Palestinian babies are not innocent civilians but "terrorists" who should be killed, that more infrastructure in Gaza needs to be destroyed, and that "It would be better if you kill all the terrorists and kill everyone who are supporters."<ref>{{cite magazine |last=Otten |first=Tori |date=1 February 2024 |title=GOP Congressman Says Dead Palestinian Babies Aren't All That Innocent |url=https://newrepublic.com/post/178679/gop-congressman-brian-mast-dead-palestinian-babies-not-innocent |access-date=3 February 2024 |magazine=[[The New Republic]] |issn=0028-6583 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240201235221/https://newrepublic.com/post/178679/gop-congressman-brian-mast-dead-palestinian-babies-not-innocent |archive-date=1 February 2024}}</ref>

In an interview with [[Fox News]] on March 5, 2024, the former president and presumptive Republican presidential candidate [[Donald Trump]] stated that [[Joe Biden]] "dumped Israel" due to being overly influenced by pro-Palestinian protests, that "The Democrats are very bad for Israel," that he supports Israel’s ongoing offensive on Gaza in which Israel has to "finish the problem", and that the Biden administration "got soft", which commentators has viewed as a call to continue and "double down" on genocidal acts. Trump's campaign also said that, if elected again, he would bar Gaza residents from entering the U.S. as part of an expanded travel ban.<ref>{{bulleted list|

In a [[town hall]] meeting on March 25, 2024, the [[Republican Party (United States)|Republican]] [[US House]] representative [[Tim Walberg]] of [[Michigan]] stated that Palestinian civilians should have nuclear weapons used against them, "like [[Nagasaki]] and [[Hiroshima]]" (the Japanese cities where the US dropped atomic bombs at the end of [[World War Two]], killing hundreds of thousands of people) in order to "Get it over quick."<ref name="TimWalbergNuclearGenocide1">{{cite news |url=https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2024/mar/31/tim-walberg-republican-congressman-gaza |title=Congressman rebuked for call to bomb Gaza 'like Nagasaki and Hiroshima' |first=Ramon Antonio |last=Vargas |work=[[The Guardian]] |date=31 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240713180328/https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2024/mar/31/tim-walberg-republican-congressman-gaza |archive-date=13 July 2024}}</ref><ref name="TimWalbergNuclearGenocide2">{{cite news |url=https://edition.cnn.com/2024/03/31/politics/tim-walberg-gaza-nagasaki-hiroshima/index.html |title=GOP congressman appears to suggest dropping bombs on Gaza to end conflict quickly, referring to 'Nagasaki and Hiroshima' |first=Sam |last=Fossum |work=[[CNN]] |date=31 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240522170724/https://edition.cnn.com/2024/03/31/politics/tim-walberg-gaza-nagasaki-hiroshima/index.html |archive-date=22 May 2024}}</ref><ref name="TimWalbergNuclearGenocide3">{{cite news |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2024/03/31/us/politics/tim-walberg-gaza-nagasaki-hiroshima.html |title=Republican Congressman Says of Gaza: 'It Should Be Like Nagasaki and Hiroshima' |first=Neil |last=Vigdor |work=[[The New York Times]] |date=31 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240701182604/https://www.nytimes.com/2024/03/31/us/politics/tim-walberg-gaza-nagasaki-hiroshima.html |archive-date=1 July 2024}}</ref>

A group of eight [[Democratic Party (United States)|Democrat]] Senators led by [[Bernie Sanders]], [[Jeff Merkley]], and [[Chris Van Hollen]] issued an official letter to President Joe Biden, calling on him to "enforce federal law" by requiring Israel's Prime Minister Benjamin Netanyahu "to stop restricting humanitarian aid access to Gaza or forfeit U.S. military aid to Israel" as "The severe humanitarian catastrophe unfolding in Gaza is nearly unprecedented in modern history" and "The United States should not provide military assistance to any country that interferes with U.S. humanitarian assistance." They cited the 1961 [[Foreign Assistance Act]], which states that "no assistance" shall be provided under that law or the [[Arms Export Control Act]] to any country that restricts, directly or indirectly, the transport or delivery of U.S. humanitarian assistance. "Stopping American humanitarian aid is in violation of the law. That should be clear. No more money to [[Benjamin Netanyahu|Netanyahu's]] war machine to kill Palestinian children," Sanders said.<ref>{{bulleted list|
|{{cite web |url=https://www.upi.com/Top_News/US/2024/03/12/Sanders-Biden-Netanyahu-Gaza/1231710262900/ |title=Bernie Sanders leads Democrats in call for Joe Biden to ensure aid reaches Gaza |first=Chris |last=Benson |website=[[United Press International]] |date=12 March 2024 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240728035635/https://www.upi.com/Top_News/US/2024/03/12/Sanders-Biden-Netanyahu-Gaza/1231710262900/ |archive-date=28 July 2024}}

===Other states===
On 8 January 2024, Jordanian foreign minister [[Ayman Safadi]] condemned Israel's actions in Gaza, stating, "The Israeli aggression on Gaza has exceeded all humanitarian, legal and moral limits".<ref>{{cite web |date= |title=Safadi condemns Israeli aggression on Gaza, criticises Security Council inaction |url=http://www.jordantimes.com/news/local/safadi%C2%A0condemns%C2%A0israeli-aggression-gaza-criticises%C2%A0security-council-inaction |website=The Jordan Times |access-date=8 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240204051459/http://www.jordantimes.com/news/local/safadi%C2%A0condemns%C2%A0israeli-aggression-gaza-criticises%C2%A0security-council-inaction |archive-date=4 February 2024}}</ref>

water supplies to Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |first=Hamish |last=Morrison |title=David Cameron squirms as he's confronted over Israeli 'war crimes' An impending [[Rafah offensive|Israeli offensive]] will displace millions."<ref>{{cite news |date=18 February 2024 |title=UAE calls for immediate ceasefire and aid to Gaza |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/2/18/israels-war-on-gaza-live-palestinians-fleeing-rafah-face-israeli-strikes?update=2716642 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=19 February 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240219050037/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2024/2/18/israels-war-on-gaza-live-palestinians-fleeing-rafah-face-israeli-strikes?update=2716642 |archive-date=19 February 2024}}</ref>

Speaking about [[Rafah]], a German government spokesperson stated on 19 February 2024 that although the full scope of the crisis was difficult to assess, "Everyone recognizes that it is catastrophic."<ref>{{cite news |date=19 February 2024 |title=German government deeply concerned about planned Rafah offensive |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/german-government-deeply-concerned-about-planned-rafah-offensive/ |work=[[Times of Israel]] |agency=[[Reuters]] |access-date=21 February 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240221011137/https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/german-government-deeply-concerned-about-planned-rafah-offensive/ |archive-date=21 February 2024}}</ref> [[William, Prince of Wales]] stated, "There is a desperate need for increased humanitarian support to Gaza."<ref>{{cite magazine |last1=Syed |first1=Armani |date=20 February 2024 |title=Prince William Calls for End to Fighting in Gaza 'as Soon as Possible' in Rare Statement |url=https://time.com/6696660/prince-william-gaza/ |magazine=[[Time (magazine)|Time]] |access-date=21 February 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240225203857/https://time.com/6696660/prince-william-gaza/ |archive-date=25 February 2024}}</ref> On 3 March, France’s Foreign Minister [[Stéphane Séjourné]] stated, "The humanitarian situation in Gaza has been catastrophic for several weeks, if not several months. And this is creating indefensible and unjustifiable situations for which the Israelis are accountable".<ref>{{cite news |title=French foreign minister: 'The humanitarian situation in Gaza is creating indefensible and unjustifiable situations for which the Israelis are accountable' |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/en/international/article/2024/03/02/french-foreign-minister-the-humanitarian-situation-in-gaza-is-creating-indefensible-and-unjustifiable-situations-for-which-the-israelis-are-accountable_6578352_4.html#:~:text=The%20humanitarian%20situation%20in%20Gaza%20has%20been%20catastrophic%20for%20several,Israel%20needs%20to%20hear%20this. |newspaper=[[Le Monde]] | date=2 March 2024 |access-date=4 March 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240723044252/https://www.lemonde.fr/en/international/article/2024/03/02/french-foreign-minister-the-humanitarian-situation-in-gaza-is-creating-indefensible-and-unjustifiable-situations-for-which-the-israelis-are-accountable_6578352_4.html |archive-date=23 July 2024}}</ref> On 26 March, the German foreign minister [[Anna Baerbock]] stated, "The humanitarian situation in Gaza is hell".<ref>{{cite news |last1=More |first1=Rachel |title=Germany's Baerbock calls for unhindered flow of aid to Gaza |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/germanys-baerbock-calls-unhindered-flow-aid-gaza-2024-03-26/#:~:text=%22The%20humanitarian%20situation%20in%20Gaza,with%20Israeli%20and%20Palestinian%20officials. |work=[[Reuters]] |access-date=29 March 2024 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240731101145/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/germanys-baerbock-calls-unhindered-flow-aid-gaza-2024-03-26/ |archive-date=31 July 2024}}</ref>

===Resolution efforts===
In a call on 20 November, Chinese President [[Xi Jinping]] and French President [[Emmanuel Macron]] discussed measures to avoid the humanitarian crisis from getting worse.<ref>{{cite news |title=Xi, Macron Discuss Israel-Hamas War In Call: State Media |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/xi-macron-discuss-israel-hamas-war-in-call-state-media-f50d4375 |magazine=[[Barron's]] |agency=[[Agence France-Presse]] |access-date=20 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231215214949/https://www.barrons.com/news/xi-macron-discuss-israel-hamas-war-in-call-state-media-f50d4375 |archive-date=15 December 2023}}</ref> In Riyadh, Saudi Arabia on November 11, 2023, the [[Organisation of Islamic Cooperation]] and the [[Arab League]] held an [[Arab Islamic extraordinary summit 2023|emergency meeting on the Gaza humanitarian crisis]] created by the war.<ref>{{cite news |date=11 November 2023 |title=Arab, Muslim leaders slam Israel at Saudi-hosted summit on Gaza |url=https://english.alarabiya.net/News/saudi-arabia/2023/11/11/Extraordinary-joint-Islamic-Arab-summit-on-Gaza-conflict-kicks-off-in-Saudi-Arabia |work=[[Al Arabiya English]] |access-date=24 November 2023 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240731104517/https://english.alarabiya.net/News/saudi-arabia/2023/11/11/Extraordinary-joint-Islamic-Arab-summit-on-Gaza-conflict-kicks-off-in-Saudi-Arabia |archive-date=31 July 2024}}</ref> On 5 December, Cyprus President [[Nikos Christodoulides]] visited Egypt and Jordan in attempt to establish a humanitarian aid corridor to Gaza.<ref>{{Cite news |date=4 December 2023 |title=Cyprus pushes Gaza corridor idea; leader to visit Egypt, Jordan |language=en |work=[[Reuters]] |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/cyprus-pushes-gaza-corridor-idea-leader-visit-egypt-jordan-2023-12-04/ |access-date=5 December 2023 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20231205013041/https://www.reuters.com/world/cyprus-pushes-gaza-corridor-idea-leader-visit-egypt-jordan-2023-12-04/ |archive-date=5 December 2023}}</ref> The UN appointed [[Sigrid Kaag]] in the newly created position of senior humanitarian and reconstruction coordinator for Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |date=9 January 2024 |title=Dutch diplomat Sigrid Kaag takes up post as UN Gaza humanitarian, reconstruction coordinator |url=https://global.chinadaily.com.cn/a/202401/09/WS659ca546a3105f21a507b461.html |work=[[China Daily]] |agency=[[Xinhua]] |access-date=10 January 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240110023734/https://global.chinadaily.com.cn/a/202401/09/WS659ca546a3105f21a507b461.html |archive-date=10 January 2024}}</ref>

On December 6, [[United Nations]] [[Secretary-General of the United Nations|secretary-general]] [[António Guterres]] invoked Article 99 of the [[Charter of the United Nations|UN Charter]], that is: "The Secretary-General may bring to the attention of the Security Council any matter which in his opinion may threaten the maintenance of international peace and security."<ref>{{Cite web |date=12 July 2023 |title=Repertory of Practice of United Nations Organs — Codification Division Publications |url=https://legal.un.org/repertory/art99.shtml |access-date=8 December 2023 |website=legal.un.org |publisher=[[United Nations]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240715045232/https://legal.un.org/repertory/art99.shtml |archive-date=15 July 2024}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=Nichols |first=Michelle |date=7 December 2023 |title=UN chief rings alarm bell on global security threat from Gaza war |language=en |work=[[Reuters]] |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/un-chief-rings-alarm-bell-global-security-threat-gaza-war-2023-12-06/ |access-date=8 December 2023 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20231206211450/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/un-chief-rings-alarm-bell-global-security-threat-gaza-war-2023-12-06/ |archive-date=6 December 2023}}</ref> Guterres cited the situation as a threat to "international peace and security" and "a severe risk of collapse of the humanitarian system" which he argued have irreversible impacts for Palestinians.<ref>{{Cite web |date=6 December 2023 |title=Gaza: Guterres invokes 'most powerful tool' Article 99, in bid for humanitarian ceasefire |url=https://news.un.org/en/story/2023/12/1144447 |access-date=8 December 2023 |website=UN News |publisher=[[United Nations]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240603003103/https://news.un.org/en/story/2023/12/1144447 |archive-date=3 June 2024}}</ref> By invoking Article 99, Guterres is pushing the [[United Nations Security Council|Security Council]] to call for a cease fire.<ref>{{Cite news |date=7 December 2023 |title=UN secretary-general invokes Article 99 on Gaza in rare, powerful move |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/12/7/un-secretary-general-invokes-article-99-on-gaza |access-date=28 December 2023 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |language=en |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240712195420/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/12/7/un-secretary-general-invokes-article-99-on-gaza |archive-date=12 July 2024}}</ref>

=== Refugees ===
At the beginning of the war, [[Egypt]] announced it was closing the [[Rafah Crossing]] to Gaza, one of only three exit points along the Gaza border.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Al-Kassab |first1=Fatima |date=7 November 2023 |title=What is Gaza's Rafah crossing and why is it important? |url=https://www.npr.org/2023/11/07/1210897789/rafah-crossing-gaza-egypt-israel-hamas-war |work=[[NPR]] |access-date=11 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240605205316/https://www.npr.org/2023/11/07/1210897789/rafah-crossing-gaza-egypt-israel-hamas-war |archive-date=5 June 2024}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Farrell |first1=Stephen |title=Who controls the Rafah crossing and why is it so important to Gaza? |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/why-gazas-rafah-border-crossing-matters-why-egypt-is-keeping-it-shut-2023-10-17/ |work=[[Reuters]] |date=November 2023 |access-date=11 November 2023 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20231017152452/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/why-gazas-rafah-border-crossing-matters-why-egypt-is-keeping-it-shut-2023-10-17/ |archive-date=17 October 2023}}</ref> Egypt cited fears about [[Forced displacement|permanent displacement]] and a possible [[refugee crisis]], particularly if Israel refused to allow the refugees back into Gaza after the war.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Gbadamosi |first1=Nosmot |title=Why Egypt Won't Open Its Border With Gaza |url=https://foreignpolicy.com/2023/10/18/egypt-hamas-israel-border-gaza/ |work=[[Foreign Policy]] |date=18 October 2023 |access-date=11 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240302050918/https://foreignpolicy.com/2023/10/18/egypt-hamas-israel-border-gaza/ |archive-date=2 March 2024}}</ref>{{efn|On 2 November, Egypt said it would allow 7,000 dual citizens to exit through the [[Rafah Border Crossing|Rafah border crossing]].<ref>{{Cite news |last=Carroll |first=Rory |date=2 November 2023 |title=Egypt says it will help evacuate about 7,000 foreign passport holders from Gaza |language=en-GB |work=[[The Guardian]] |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/nov/02/joe-biden-urges-pause-gaza-fighting-hamas-jabalia-refugee-camp-death-toll |access-date=2 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240114163149/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/nov/02/joe-biden-urges-pause-gaza-fighting-hamas-jabalia-refugee-camp-death-toll |archive-date=14 January 2024}}</ref>}} Israeli PM [[Benjamin Netanyahu]] sought to convince Egypt to accept Gazan refugees.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Foy |first1=Henry |last2=Abboud |first2=Leila |last3=Mancini |first3=Donato Paolo |last4=England |first4=Andrew |title=Israel's Netanyahu lobbied EU to pressure Egypt into accepting Gaza refugees |url=https://www.ft.com/content/75971d8b-e2fd-4275-8747-0bd443673483 |work=[[Financial Times]] |date=30 October 2023 |access-date=11 November 2023 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20231102214703/https://www.ft.com/content/75971d8b-e2fd-4275-8747-0bd443673483 |archive-date=2 November 2023}}</ref>

[[Jordan]] also expressed reluctance to receive Palestinian refugees.<ref name=thehill20231018>{{cite news |first=Lauren |last=Irwin |date=18 October 2023 |title=Scotland's first minister says country willing to take Gaza refugees |url=https://thehill.com/policy/international/4262981-scotlands-first-minister-says-country-willing-to-take-gaza-refugees/ |work=[[The Hill (newspaper)|The Hill]] |access-date=27 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240501223148/https://thehill.com/policy/international/4262981-scotlands-first-minister-says-country-willing-to-take-gaza-refugees/ |archive-date=1 May 2024}}</ref> King [[Abdullah II of Jordan]] warned Israel against pushing Palestinians into Jordan, emphasizing the need to address the humanitarian situation within both Gaza and the [[West Bank]].<ref>{{cite news |first=Safaa |last=Kasraoui |title=King of Jordan on Palestine: 'No Refugees in Jordan, No Refugees in Egypt' |date=17 October 2023 |url=https://www.moroccoworldnews.com/2023/10/358370/king-of-jordan-on-palestine-no-refugees-in-jordan-no-refugees-in-egypt |work=Morocco World News |access-date=27 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231027063446/https://www.moroccoworldnews.com/2023/10/358370/king-of-jordan-on-palestine-no-refugees-in-jordan-no-refugees-in-egypt |archive-date=27 October 2023}}</ref>

In Europe, [[Humza Yousaf]], the [[First Minister of Scotland]], urged the international community to establish a refugee program for Gaza.<ref>{{cite news |first=Neil |last=Murphy |date=17 October 2023 |title=Scotland's First Minister Humza Yousaf says UK should offer sanctuary for Gaza refugees |url=https://www.thenationalnews.com/world/uk-news/2023/10/17/scotlands-first-minister-humza-yousaf-says-uk-should-offer-sanctuary-for-gaza-refugees/ |work=[[The National (Abu Dhabi)|The National]] |access-date=27 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240718085200/https://www.thenationalnews.com/world/uk-news/2023/10/17/scotlands-first-minister-humza-yousaf-says-uk-should-offer-sanctuary-for-gaza-refugees/ |archive-date=18 July 2024}}</ref><ref name="Willing to be a place of sanctuary">{{cite news |date=18 October 2023 |title='Willing to be a place of sanctuary': Scotland First Minister says ready to welcome Gaza refugees |url=https://www.businesstoday.in/latest/world/story/willing-to-be-a-place-of-sanctuary-scotland-first-minister-says-ready-to-welcome-gaza-refugees-402497-2023-10-18 |work=BI |access-date=27 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231105231857/https://www.businesstoday.in/latest/world/story/willing-to-be-a-place-of-sanctuary-scotland-first-minister-says-ready-to-welcome-gaza-refugees-402497-2023-10-18 |archive-date=5 November 2023}}</ref> Yousaf stated Scotland was ready to offer sanctuary to refugees, and called on the UK to create a resettlement scheme.<ref name="Willing to be a place of sanctuary"/>{{efn|Yousaf also called on Israel not to resort to collective punishment and emphasized the need for medical evacuation support for injured civilians. Yousaf has personal ties to Gaza, with family members there. He stressed unity and safety for all communities in Scotland. The UK government, led by conservative [[Rishi Sunak]], did not issue an official response to Yousaf's comments.}} Foreign Minister [[Hanke Bruins Slot]] stated the Netherlands was discussing the possibility of accepting sick and wounded Palestinian children into the country.<ref>{{cite news |first=Joseph |last=Stepansky |date=13 November 2023 |title=Dutch foreign minister says her country 'discussing' bringing wounded Palestinian children to Netherlands |url=https://aje.io/jui07c?update=2483866 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=14 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240324114748/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2023/11/13/israel-hamas-war-live-gazas-two-largest-hospitals-shut-amid-nonstop-raids?update=2483866 |archive-date=24 March 2024}}</ref>

In the [[United States]], left-wing politicians, including Representatives [[Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez]] and [[Jamaal Bowman]], emphasized the US's historical role accepting refugees and called for the acceptance of Gazan refugees.<ref name=thehill20231018 /> Right-wing politicians, such as former-President [[Donald Trump]] and Governor [[Ron DeSantis]], both argued for barring admittance of any refugees from Gaza.<ref name=thehill20231018 /> Former US ambassador to the UN, [[Nikki Haley]], said that [[Palestinian refugees]] from Gaza should be accepted by Middle Eastern countries.<ref>{{cite news |last=Suter |first=Tara |title=Haley argues Middle Eastern nations should take Gaza refugees |url=https://thehill.com/homenews/campaign/4260755-haley-middle-east-should-take-gaza-refugees/ |work=[[The Hill (newspaper)|The Hill]] |date=17 October 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240301125135/https://thehill.com/homenews/campaign/4260755-haley-middle-east-should-take-gaza-refugees/ |archive-date=1 March 2024}}</ref> President [[Joe Biden]] did not announce any plans to admit refugees, but stated $100 million in [[aid]] would be given to Gaza.<ref name=thehill20231018 />
